TC_11.9^2	 acāra kartavyatā anumānayoḥ anādi tvena ācārāṇām kartavyatva anumāna mūlaka tvāt na andha paramparā na ca pūrva anumāna sāpekṣam uttara anumānam iti svatantra pramāṇa mūlaka tva abhāvāt sā vyāpti pakṣa dharma tāvat tvena sarveṣām svatantra pramāṇa tvāt na api itara prāmānya adhīnam sarvasya prāmāṇyam iti na nirapekṣa tvam pratyakṣa ādeḥ api tathā tva āpatteḥ etena vivāda padam ācāraḥ nirapekṣa pramāṇa mūlakaḥ avigīta mahā janā jāra tvāt pratyakṣa veda mūla ācāra vat iti nirastam anumānasya nirapekṣa pramaṇa tvāt pramāṇa mūla tvanā eva hetoḥ upapatteḥ nirapekṣa tvasya gauraveṇa aprayojaka tvāt ca 
TC_11.9^3	 na ca sa apekṣa tvena na pramāṇatā vyāpti ādi sattvāt na ca sa apekṣa tvena na pramāṇatā vyāpti ādi sattvāt  anyathā pramāṇe nairapekṣasya vaiyarthyāt na ca ācāre veda mūla tva prasiddheḥ tad anumānam asiddheḥ vyabhicārāt anyathā upapatteḥ ca na ca veda mūla tvena eva mahājana parigrahāt tathā na hi veda mūlaḥ ayam iti kṛtvā mahājanānām tad parigrahaḥ veda mūla tvasya prathamam jñātum aśakyatvāt śakya tve vā kim anumānena na ca veda mūla tvena eva mahājana parigṛhītaḥ ayam ācāraḥ iti jñātvā tatra mahā jana parigrahaḥ gauravāt asiddheḥ ca pūrva mahā jana parigrahāt eva uttarottareṣām parigrahāt anuṣṭhāna upapatteḥ 
TC_11.9^4	 tādṛśa smṛti ācārayoḥ veda mala tvena vyāpteḥ veda siddhiḥ iti ced na asambhavat mūla antara tvasya upādhi tvāt anyathā lobha nyāya mūla smṛteḥ api veda mūla tva prasaṅgaḥ astu vā smṛti ācārayoḥ anādi tvam na ca ācārāt smṛtiḥ smṛteḥ ācāraḥ iti andha paramparā mūla bhūta pramāṇa abhāvāt iti vacyam smṛti ācārayoḥ ubhayoḥ api pramāṇa tvāt anyathā na tatas veda anumānam api iti ucyate pralaye pūrva smṛti ācārayoḥ ucchedāt sarga ādau nitya sarva jñeśvara praṇīta veda mūla tvam smṛti ācārayoḥ anyathā mūla abhāvena andha paramparā prasaṅgaḥ na ca manu ādīnām atīndriya artha darśi tvam tad upāya śravaṇa ādeḥ tadānīm abhavāt 
TC_11.9^5	 pūrva sarga siddha sarvajñam anu ādayaḥ eva te iti ced na pramāṇa abhāvāt smṛti ācārayoḥ pramāṇa mūla tvam eva tat kalpanam iti ced na pratisargam teṣām anyonya tva kalpane gauravam iti ekasya eva nitya sarvajñasya kalpanāt na ca smṛtayaḥ eva tad praṇītāḥ tāsām manu ādi kartṛka tvena smṛtau bodhanāt smṛtau= eva smṛtīnām veda mūla tva smaraṇāñca evañca smṛti ācārayoḥ mahājana parigrahāt veda mūla tva sādhakam api bhagavati pramāṇam atas eva pratimanvantarañcā eṣā śrutiḥ anyā vidhīyate iti āgamaḥ api 
TC_11.9^6	 evañca pūrvam pratyakṣa mūlau= eva smṛti ācārau agre ca kāla krameṇa āyuḥ ārogya bala śraddhā grahaṇa dhāraṇa ādi śakteḥ aharapacīyamāna tvāt tad adhyayana vicchedana śākhā ucchedāt smṛtyācārabhyām eva kartavyatām adhigatya pravṛttiḥ nanu evam smṛtiḥ aḥ tu veda mūlā maṅgala ādi a ācāraḥ tu īśvarāt eva bhaviṣyati ghaṭa lipya ādi samprādaya vat iti ced na bahu vyāpāra ghaṭitasya tat tad ācārasya guru tvena maṅgalam ācaret ityādi vākyasya eva lāghavena kalpanāt na ca maṅgala ādi pada śakti graha arthe tad upapatteḥ atas eva yatra vacana mātrāt para pratipattiḥ tatra na ācāraḥ parīkṣakāṇām tasya ca veda tvam na īśvara praṇīta tvena śakti grahaṇa artha tad vacane vyabhicārāt kintu tādṛśa ācāra asya veda mūla tva niyamāt iti 
TC_11.9^7	 syādet pralaye sati evam eva tat saḥ eva tu na asti pramāṇa abhāvat iti ced na kāla kapālāni āvṛtti ghaṭa prāgabhāvaḥ kārya dravya anādhāra ādhāraḥ kārya dravya an adhikaraṇa kārya adhikaraṇa vṛttiḥ vā abhāva tvāt ākāśa vṛtti anyonya abhāva vat iti vṛtta pralaya sādhanāt evam eva ghaṭa dhvaṃsam pakṣīkṛtya āgāmi pralaya sādhanam yat vā ghaṭaḥ kārya dravya an adhikaraṇa kārya adhikaraṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyogī kāryatvāt śabda vat yat vā kārya dravya tvam kārya dravyān adhikaraṇa kārya adhikaraṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyogi vṛtti kārya mātra vṛtti tvāt śabda tva vat yat vā eka kālīnāḥ sarve paramāṇavaḥ samagrīpādeya prabandha śūnyāḥ ārambhaka tvāt naṣṭa pavana ārambhaka paramāṇu vat 
TC_11.9^8	 sarvatra pakṣa tā avacchedaka avacchinnam sādhyam pratīyate iti eka kāle śūnyate labhyate na ca pavana parama aṇūnām api pakṣa tvena aṃśataḥ siddha sādhanam pakṣa dharmatā bala labhya sādhya apratīteḥ abheda anumāna vat ca pakṣasya dṛṣṭānta tva avirodhaḥ yat vā paramāṇavaḥ kārya dravyān adhikaraṇa vṛtti kāryavantaḥ nitya dravya tvāt ākāśa vat bhū golaka santānaḥ ayam bhū golaka santānān adhikaraṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyogī kāryatvāt ghaṭa vat yat vā etat karma atiktāni karmāṇi etad pratibandhaka pratibadhyāni karma tvāt etat karma vat na ca atra vyabhicāra śaṅkā sarveṣām evaṃrūpa tvāt anevambhāve ca svabhāva pracyavāt anyathā niyame api niyama antara apekṣāyām anavasthiteḥ āgamaḥ api amum eva artham saṃvata di iti kṛtam prasakta anuprasaktyā 
TC_12.1^1	 ācāra mūla tvam vedasya pravartaka jñāna janaka tvena bhavati iti pravartaka jñānam nirūpyate tatra abhidhā saṅkalpa apūrva bhāvanā jñānam na pravartakam tasmin sati api apravṛtteḥ asati api pravṛtteḥ ca kāryatva jñānam pravartakam iti guravaḥ tathā hi jñānasya kṛtau janyāyām cikīrṣā atiriktam na kartavyam asti tad sattve kṛti vilambaḥ hetu antara abhāvāt cikīrṣā ca kṛti sādhya tva prakārikā kṛti sādhya kriyā viṣaya icchā pākam kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti tad anubhavāt sā ca sva kṛti sādhya tā jñāna sādhyāḥ icchāyāḥ sva prakāraka dhī sādhya tva niyamāt 
TC_12.1^2–12.2	 atas eva sva kṛti sādhye pāke pravartate na tu iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna sādhyā sva kṛtya sadhye cikīrṣā patteḥ sva kṛti asādhya tva jñānam pratibandhakam iti ced na tad abhāva kāraṇa tve gauravāt atha abhāvaḥ ubhaya siddhaḥ kṛti sādhya ta adhīra siddhā iti atas na lāghava avasaraḥ iti ced na yatra śabdāt anumānadvā daivāt sā tatra lāghava avatārāt icchāyāḥ sva prakāraka jñāna sādhya tva niyamena kṛti sādhya tva jñānasya āvaśyaka tvāt ca janaka jñānam vighaṭayate eva jñānasya pratibandhaka tvāt ca vyāpti jñāna vighaṭana dvārāḥ anumiti pratibandhaka anaikāntika jñāna vat anyathā sva kṛti asādhya tva aniṣṭa sādhanatva upekṣaṇī tva niṣphala tva jñānam pratibandhakam kriyā jñānam eva pravartakam kalpeta 
TC_12.3^1	 nanu sanaḥ dhātu artha gocara icchā vāci tvāt lāghavāñca kṛtau= icchā cikīrṣā sā ca vṛṣṭauviva iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt iti ced na vahninā sādhayāmi iti vat kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchāyāḥ kṛteḥ pūrvam anubhūyamānāyāḥ sanantā vācya tvena gauraveṇa ca pratyākhyātum aśakya tvāt kiñca pākam cikīrṣati iti atra prādhānyena pākasya icchā viṣaya tvam anubhūyate na tu kṛteḥ dhātoḥ ca san pratyaya abhidheya icchā prakāra vāci tvam odanam bubhukṣate iti atra bhojana viśeṣya tayā odanasya icchā viṣayatva anubhavāt iṣṭa sādhana tvena vṛṣṭau= iva kṛtau= icchā sambhave api kṛtīcchā na pravartikā kintu sva kṛti sādhya icśā eva ghaṭam jānāti cikīrṣati karotī jñāna cikīrṣā kṛtīnām eka viṣaya tva anubhavāt atha yadi kṛtyā sādhayitum icchā sā tadā cikīrṣitasya pākasya anyatas siddhau sā na apagacchet na hi upāya viśeṣa sādhya tvena icchā upāya antara adhīna phala lābhena nivāryate prītyā dhana lābhe api pratigraheṇa tad lipsāyāḥ anivṛtteḥ iti ced na sva viṣaya siddha tvasya phala icchā vicchedasya ca upāya icchā virodha tvāt 
TC_12.3^2	 asti ca tatra pāka odanayoḥ siddhatvam anya odana icchāyām pāka cikīrṣā bhavati eva pratyuta asiddha tvāt kṛtau= eva icchā na vicchidyeta yadi kṛti viṣaya siddha tva phala icchā vicchedau na virodhinau prītyā dhana lābhe ca tad adhika dhana icchā na vicchidyate tasya asiddha tvāt tad phala icchāyāḥ ca sattvāt dhana mātra arthinaḥ ca prītyā dhana lābhe api pratigraheṇa tad lipsā na asti eva dhana mātrasya siddha tvāt kiñcid viśeṣa siddhyā eva hi sāmānya it chā vicchedaḥ anyathā sakala sva viṣaya siddheḥ asambhavena tad vicchedaḥ na syāt eva vastutas tu kriyā anukūlā kṛtiḥ iṣṭa upāyaḥ iti jñāne kriyāyāḥ kṛti sādhya tvam iṣṭa upāya tvañca bhātam kriyā dvārā eva kṛteḥ iṣṭa sādhana tvāt iti tad bodhāt kṛtau= iva kṛti sādhya tvena kriyāyām api sā eva icchā iti cikīrṣāyām kṛti sādhya tva prakāra naiyatyam atas kṛti samāna viṣaya cikīrṣā tvena cikīrṣāyāḥ kṛti kāraṇa tvam na tu kṛti icchā tvena bhinna viṣaya tayā gauravāt 
TC_12.3^3	 tathā api yena rūpeṇa yasya iṣṭa sādhana tvam tena prakāreṇa tatra icchā yathā sva kedāra vṛṣṭi tvena iṣṭa sādhana tvāt tathā eva aicchā tathā kṛti sādhya tvena pākasya iṣṭa sā adhana tvam atas kṛti sādhya tvena tatra icchā bhavati iti kṛtau kṛti viṣaye vā cikīrṣāyām na vṛṣṭī icchā vilakṣaṇa sāmagrayantara kalpanam iti ced bhavet evam yadi kṛti sādhya tvena pākasya odana sādhana tā syāt na ca evam gauravāt kintu pāka tvena sa tu kṛtim vinā na iti anyat etat vahninā sādhayāmi iti vat kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt eva iti ced tarhi tatra vahni sādhya tā jñāna vat atra api kṛti sādhya tva jñānam kāraṇam āvaśyakam kṛtau ca anubhava siddha cikīrṣā adhīnata tvam viśeṣaḥ tena prāṇa pañcaka sañcāre jīvana yoni kṛti sādhye na pravṛttiḥ anyathā kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api tatra pravarteta 
TC_12.3^4	 nanu cikīrṣā adhīna tvasya upalakṣaṇa tve upalakṣya mātra gata anati prasakta dharma abhāvāt kṛti mātrasya ca atiprasaṅgāt tad tad kṛti viśeṣāḥ upalakṣyāḥ tathā ca tad ananugamāt pravṛtti ananugamaḥ viśeṣaṇa tve cikīrṣāyām pravṛttau ca cikīrṣā jñāna kāraṇa tve gauravam pramāṇa abhāvaḥ ca kiñca cikīrṣā asādhya avasthāyāḥ kṛteḥ siddha avastha sādhana tva virodhena kṛti sādhya tā pāka ādau na jñāyeta iti ced na asti hi kṛti viśeṣaḥ mānasa pratyakṣa siddhaḥ jīvana yoni prayatna vyāvṛttaḥ cikīrṣā upalakṣyaḥ yatra cikīrṣā kāraṇa tva grahaḥ sa ca tava jāti rūpaḥ mama tu anugata kāraṇa upādhi rūpaḥ evañca cikīrṣā adhīna tvena anugatena kṛti viśeṣāṇām upalakṣyāṇām anugata tvam api yathā go tveṇa taṭa sthe na upalakṣitāḥ mahiṣī ādi vyāvṛtta dhāna karma vyakti viśeṣāḥ 
TC_12.4^1	 dhenupadena ucyate na tu go tvam api tathā cikīrṣā api evam jīvana yoni yatna vyāvṛtta kṛti viśeṣāṇām kṛti tvena jñānam kāraṇam iti na ananugamaḥ nanu kṛti sādhye na kṛtiḥ viśeṣaṇam asattvāt sattve vā kṛtau satyām jñānam jñāne ca kṛtiḥ iti anyonya āśrayaḥ na upalakṣaṇam ati prasaṅgāt iti ced na kṛtiḥ hi jñāne viṣaya tayā viśeṣaṇam eva sādhye ca paricāyaka tayā upalakṣaṇam anyathā iṣṭa sādhane api iṣṭam na viśeṣaṇam asattvāt na upalakṣaṇam ati prasaṅgāt liṅga jñāna ādau vā kā gatiḥ nanu evam śrame api cikīrṣā syāt tasya api cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti sādhya tvāt atra vadanti 
TC_12.4^2	 śramaḥ tu bhojana ādi kriyā sādhyaḥ na tad kṛti sādhyaḥ acikīrṣita tvāt kṛteḥ sva dhvaṃsa sākṣātkāra atirikte cikīrṣā viṣaya mātre janaka tvāt na hi bhojana cikīrṣā viṣaya mātre janaka tvāt na hi bhojana cikīrṣā adhīna kṛtyā gamanam sādhyate iti kecid tat na gurutara bhāra uttolane kṛtya sādhye bhramāt pravṛttasya nigaḍa niścala dehasya vā kṛtau satyām uttolana calana kriyā anutpāde api śrama anubhavāt kṛteḥ eva kāraṇa tvāt na tu tad janya kriyāyāḥ sukhe vyabhicārāt ca na hi sukham kṛti kāraṇa cikīrṣā viṣayaḥ upāya cikīrṣā janyā hi kṛtiḥ na tu sukha cikīrṣā janyā cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhya tvam na śrame dveṣa yoni prayatnāt api tad utpatteḥ iti apare tat na śatru badhasya iṣṭa sā ādhatana tvena cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhya tvāt dveṣasya yatna ajanaka tvāt dveṣa siddhiḥ tu śatrum dveṣmi iti anubhava balāt 
TC_12.5^1	 yat tu śramaḥ kṛti tvena kṛti sādhyaḥ na cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti tvena yadi acikīrṣi atepi śrame cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti tvena kāraṇa tā syāt tadā cikīrṣitam eva bhojanam kṛtyā sādhyate na acikīrṣitam gamana ādi iti na syāt śrama vaṅga mane api tad janya tva prasaṅgāt bhojana ādiḥ ca cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti viśeṣāt sa hi kṛti mātram vyabhicārati jīvana yokṛteḥ tad anutpādāt yat vā śramaḥ na bhojana kṛti sādhyaḥ kintu tat nirantara utpannat jīvana yoni prayatnāt eva iti tat na na hi 
TC_12.5^2	 kṛti tvena tat śrama janaka tvam na api kṛti antarāt eva śrama utpattiḥ jīvana yoni prayatne sati api bhāra udvahana ādikam akurvataḥ tādṛśa namān anubhavena tasya śrama ajanaka tvāt tasmāt bhojana ādi vat śrama viśeṣaṇām api bhojana ādi kṛti sādhya tvam ananya gatika tvāt suptasya sveda ādi anumitaḥ śramaḥ tad janyaḥ iti ced na sveda ādeḥ śramāni ahetuka tvāt anyathā jāgare api tad anuvṛttau śrama anuvṛtti prasaṅgāt iti mā evam sva icchā adhīna kṛti śeṣaṇa tvāt śramaḥ ca niyamataḥ anya icśā adhīna kṛti sādhyaḥ śrame duḥkha tvena icchā virahāt atas eva anya icchā janya kṛti sādhya tvena śramaḥ na antarīyakaḥ iti ucyate sva cikīrṣa adhīna tvantu na kṛtau viśeṣaṇam gauravāt 
TC_12.6–12.7	 anye tu kṛti gatam dharma antaram eva uddeśya tvam tad viśiṣṭa kṛti sādhyaḥ ca na śramaḥ acikīrṣita tvāt kintu kṛti mātra sādhyaḥ atas eva kaṣṭam karma iti anubhavaḥ lokānām evam cikīrṣāyām mama ekam kṛti sādhya tvam prayojakam tava tu kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tvam sukha tvam duḥkha abhāva tvañcā iti catuṣṭayam icchā prayojakantu mama sukha tvam duḥkha abhāva tvañcā iti dvayam vṛṣṭi sādhna tvena tatra icchā sādhana tvasya icchā virodhi tvāt tava tu cayam viṣa bhakṣaṇe tu kṛti sādhya tve api balavat aniṣṭa sādhana tvena cikīrṣā na asti iti kṛtau cikīrṣā janya tvam viśeṣaṇam iti kaścid tad tuccham evam hi viṣa bhakṣaṇam kṛti sādhyam eva na syāt jīvana yoni kṛte stasya anutpatteḥ iti vyartham viśeṣaṇam syāt etat iṣṭa sādhana tā bhramāt viṣa bhakṣaṇe caitya vandane ca cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhya tvam asti jñāna prayukta tvāt kāryatvasya tathā ca sañjāta bādhaḥ api tatra kāryam tu ajñānāt pravarteta tathā tṛptaḥ api bhojane 
TC_12.8	 nanu sva kṛti sādhyata anubhavaḥ tathā anyathā iṣṭa sādhana tā smaraṇe viṣa bhakṣaṇe api pravarteta na ca iṣṭa sā adhana tā jñānam vedaḥ vā anubhāvakam asti iti ced na vastutas tatra kṛti sādhya tve liṅga antareṇa āpta vākyena vā tad anubhava sambhavāt liṅga ābhāsāt śabda ābhāsāt vā apravṛtti prasaṅgāt ca bheda agrahavādinaḥ tat ca tava tad anubhava abhāvāt mā evam sva viśeṣaṇa vat tā pratisandhāna janyam hi kārya tā jñānam pravartakam tathā hi kāmye puruṣa viśeṣaṇam kāmanā tatas kāmya sādhana tā jñānena yāga pāka ādau kārya tā jñānam nitye ca kāla śauca ādi sva viśeṣaṇam tathā ca etad sandhyāyām aham kṛti sādhya saṃdhyā vandanaḥ saṃdhyā samaye śauca ādi sva viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyam tat uktam sa ca kārya viśeṣaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaṇa avagataḥ pravṛtti hetuḥ iti saṃjāta bādhasya ca viṣa bhakṣaṇe caitya vandane ca bhramadaśāyām iva na iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam asti yena tad janya kārya tā jñānāt pravarteta tṛptasya ca kāmanā viraheṇa iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna abhāva na tathā bodhaḥ 
TC_12.9–12.11	 anye tu ātmanaḥ jīvitva pratisandhāna janyam śrame kṛti sādhya tā jñānam sambhavati iti jīvana vyatirikta tvam sva viśeṣaṇe viśeṣaṇam iti tat na śrame sva icchā dhīna kṛti sādhya tva abhāvāt iṣṭa sādhana tā āliṅgakam kārya tā ajñānam pravartakam iti apare tat na nitye tad abhāvāt nanu viṣa bhakṣaṇa vyāvṛttam iṣṭa sādhana tvam eva kṛti sādhyatā jñāne viṣaya tayā viśeṣaṇam astu sva viśeṣaṇa vat tā jñāna janya tva apekṣayā laghu tvāt kiñca upāya viṣayā cikīrṣā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna sādhyāḥ upāya icchā tvāt vṛṣṭī i= chāvat 
TC_12.12	 bhoga cikīrṣāyām tad abhāvau= aprayojakam iṣṭa sādhana tvam iti ced na tava api sva viśeṣaṇa dhī janya tva abhāvena tatra tasya aprayojaka tvāt kṛti hetu cikīrṣāyām tat prayojakam na ca bhoga cikīrṣā tathā upāya cikīrṣātaḥ eva kṛti sambhavāt iti ced tulyam iti mā evam sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ virodhena ekatra jñātum aśakyatvāt asiddha avasthasya hi sādhya tvam siddha tādaśāyām tad abhāvāt siddha tādaśā yāñca sādhana tvam asiddha avasthāvataḥ kārya anutpatteḥ tathā ca pāka ādeḥ asiddha tva siddha tva jñāne sādhya tva sādhana tva grahaḥ na ca ekam ekena ekadā siddha mama siddhañcaḥ iti jñāyate na ca svarūpa gatatā sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ atas na virodhaḥ iti vācyam yadi hi svarūpa nibandhanam tat ubhayam tadā tad svarūpam sadā eva siddham asiddhañca syāt bhinna nirūpita tve api tayoḥ siddha tva asiddha tve anavagamya ajñānāt tasmāt samaya bheda upādhikaḥ eva tad ubhaya sambandhaḥ pāke 
TC_12.13	 idānīm sādhya tvam agre sādhana tvam jñāyate iti ced na idānīm agrima padārthayoḥ nānā tvāt ananugamena vyāpti agrahāt śabdena tathā pratipādayitum aśakyatvāt gauravāt ca na ca kṛtitaḥ siddham iṣṭa sādhanam iti jñānāt cikīrṣā na hi siddham kaścid cikīrṣati kṛteḥ pūrva kṛtitaḥ siddham iti jñāna abhavāt ca na ca kṛti sādhya tvena pāka ādeḥ iṣṭa sādha tvāt sādhana tvam api sādhyam na hi kṛti sādhya tvena pākasya odana sādhana tā iti uktam tasmāt kṛta kriyamāṇa vilakṣaṇam kṛtī anantara bhaviṣyattā rūpam kṛti sādhya tvam cikīrṣā prayojakam tādṛśañca sādhana tva virodhyā iva kiñca sādhana tvasya siddha mātra dharma tvāt sādhana tva jñānam icchā virodhi na hi kaścid siddham icchati iti uktam etena vṛṣṭi ādā= iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam upāya it chā kāraṇa tvena kptam iti nirastam katham tarhi svatas asundare vṛṣṭi ādi vicchā tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt iti gṛhāṇa 
TC_12.14	 anye tu sukha duḥkha abhāva tad sādhana iṣṭi= chā prayojakam anugatam uddeśya tvam puruṣa artha pada vedanīyam dharma antaram asti anugata kāryasya anugata kāraṇa niyamya tvāt tat eva duḥkha tad sādhana ādau cikīrṣā prayojakam iti na ca duḥkha virodhi tvam eva tathā asti iti vācyam saha anavasthāna niyama virodhasya asambhavāt badhyadhātaka bhāvasya eka samaye samāna adhikaraṇya abhāvasya ca yatna ādi sādhāraṇyāt iti tat na tad ajñāne api sukha tva jñānāt icchotpatteḥ na hi sukha tve jñāte dharma antara jñānam vinā na icchati tathā tve svatas prayojana hāni āpatteḥ tat eva hi svatas prayojanam tat avagatam sat sva vṛttitayā iṣyate kiñca anugata dharma kalpanā api kāraṇe 
TC_12.15^1	 na ca sukha ādi icchā karaṇam anāgata tvāt kintu tad avagamaḥ tarhi sukha ādi jñāne tat sva rūpa sadeva icchā prayojakam astu iti ced na yathā hi uddeśya tvam sukha jñāna ādiṣu utpadyate anyatara tvāt tṛṇa araṇi maṇinyāyāt vā tathā eva icchā eva jāyatām kṛti sādhya tvañca kṛtau satyām agri makṣaṇe svarūpam na kṛtim vinā kṣema sādhāraṇañca etat kṛti sādhya tvañca na kṛteḥ pūrvam nanu kṛtau naṣṭāyām san= api dharmī na kāryaḥ tathā ca katham kārye apūrve kāminaḥ anvayaḥ kṣaṇika tvena kriyā tulya tvāt iti ced na yat vṛtti kāmya sādhana tvam tatra kārya tā buddheḥ prayojaka tvāt na tu kārya tā viśiṣṭasya kāmya sādhana tā iti vyāptiḥ 
TC_12.15^2	 nanu pāka ādau kṛti sādhya tā jñānam na pratyakṣeṇa kṛtī anantaram pāke sati kṛti sādhya tā jñānam tasmin sati kṛtiḥ iti anyonya āśrayāt kṛti sādhya totīrṇe cikīrṣā akṛtya uḥ asambhavāt ca iti ced na pākaḥ mad kṛti sādhyaḥ mad kṛtim vinā asattve sati mad iṣṭa sādhana tvāt daiva ādi anadhīna tve sati mad iṣṭa sādhana tvāt vā mad bhojana vat iti anumānāt sva kṛti sādhya ta ajñānam yasya yat iṣṭa sādhanam yat kṛtim vinā yadā na sambhavati tat tadā tad kati sādhyam iti vyāpteḥ asiddhasya iṣṭa sā dhana tva abhāvāt balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi tvan ca liṅga viśeṣaṇam tena na madhu viṣa saṃmpṛkta anna bhojane vyabhicāraḥ sāmānyatas tasya api kṛti sādhya totīrṇe na vyabhicāraḥ sāmānyatas tasya api kṛti sādhya tvāt atīta tā daśā yāñca atīta odana icchā viraheṇa iṣṭa sādhana tva abhāvāt atas eva nidāgha dūna deha uvarṣati vāride toyadā toya lābha sambhāvanāyām vā saraḥ avagāhane na pravartate iṣṭa santāpa śānti sādhana toya sambandhasya sva kṛtim vinā api siddhi pratisandhānena liṅga abhāvena sva kṛti sādhya tva jñāna abhāvāt yadā ca mad kṛtim vinā na sambhavati iti pratisandhatte tadā pravartate 
TC_12.16	 yasya santāpa śāntim a mātram iṣṭam sa sataḥ avagāhanasya iṣṭa sā adhana tvam eva na pratisandhatte upasthita vṛṣṭitaḥ api tad sambhavāt iti kaścid tat na toya sambandha tvena santāpa śānti sādhana tvam tasya ca saraḥ avagāhane api sattvāt anyathā vṛṣṭiḥ api tad sādhanam na syāt saraḥ avagāhanāt api tad siddheḥ kārya sādhana tvañca kṛti sādhya tve na liṅgam pāka ādi vat odana ādeḥ api pravṛtteḥ pūrvam kṛti sādhya tva jñāne hetu abhāvāt 
TC_12.17^1	 nanu evam liṅga jñānam eva pravartakam astu prāthamika tvāt āvaśyaka tvān ca na ca lāghavāt kṛti sādhya tva jñānam tathā kṛti sādhyata anumitau tadā māna abhāvena yugapad upasthiti abhāvāt pravṛtti sāmagṣa anumiti pravibandhāñca iti ced na liṅga jñāne kṛti sādhya tva aprakāśe tad prakāraka cikīrṣāyām tasya ahetu tvāt atas eva liṅga antara jñānam api na pravartakam nanu pāka ādiḥ kṛtaḥ kriyamāṇā uvā na pakṣaḥ tasya kṛti sādhya tve bādhāt na api anāgataḥ bhāvi pāke māna abhāvena āśraya asiddheḥ pāka tvam bhaviṣyat vṛtti sāmānya tvāt go tva vat iti mānam iti ced na māna abhāvena go tve api tasya aprasiddheḥ pāka mātram pakṣaḥ iti ced na mātrā arthaḥ yadi pāka tvam tadā bādholiṅga asiddhiḥ ca 
TC_12.17^2–12.18	 sarva pāka paratve ca tasya siddha bhāge bādhaḥ anāgata bhāge ca āśraya asiddhiḥ vartamāna ādi udāsīnaḥ pākaḥ pakṣaḥ pāka sāmānye ca kṛti sādhya tvam na bādhitam iti api na siddhasya pakṣa tvam na asiddhasya iti anumiteḥ siddha viṣaya tve bādhāt bhinna viṣaya tve vā siddha viṣaya icchā pravṛtti ādi anutpādaka tvāt ca kṛta kriyamāṇa sādhāraṇa kṛti sādhya tva jñānāt eva asiddha viṣayā cikīrṣā kṛtiḥ ca utpadyate ananya gatika tvena tathā kāraṇa svabhāva kalpanāt iti ced tarhi yādṛśam kṛti sādhya tvam cikīrṣāyām prakāraḥ tādṛśam jñāne na asti iti anya prakāraka jñānāt eva cikīrṣā syāt tathā ca liṅga jñānam eva pravṛtti hetuḥ astu prāthamika tvāt yat tu smṛta pāke kṛti sādhya tva asaṃsargā grahāt pravṛttiḥ sa ca asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ iṣṭa sādhana tā grahāt iti tat na smṛta pākasya siddha tvena tatra kāryatva asaṃsarga grahe anumāna bādhāt 
TC_12.19^1	 smṛta pākasya siddhatvam tadā na gṛhyate iti ced tarhi smṛta pākasya siddha tva grahe odana arthī pāke na pravarteta tatra pāka ādau siddha tva grahāt tad asaṃsarga grahaḥ iti cetulyam api ca smṛta pāke kāryatva asaṃsargāt vidyamānā saṃsarga āgrahāt visaṃvādinī pravṛttiḥ syāt kiñca evam siddha pāka jñānāt ajñāte asiddhe pāke icchā pravṛttī syātām iti atra brūmaḥ pāke kṛti sādhya tvam siddhat siddhe bādhāt anāgata pākam ādāya sidhyati pakṣa tā avacchedaka dharma sāmānādhikaraṇyam sādhyamānasya liṅgena sidhyati iti anumāne ktvāt yathā prasiddha vahni bādhe api vahni mātram na bādhitam iti aprasiddhaḥ api vahniḥ sidhyati tathā prasiddha pāke kṛti sādhya tva bādhe api pāka mātre na bādhitam iti aprasiddham pākam ādāya tat sidhyati aprasiddhayoḥ pakṣa sādhyayoḥ siddhau= aviśeṣāt tasmāt asiddhasya kvacid siddhe siddhe siddhasya ca kvacid 
TC_12.19^2	 aprasiddhasya ca asiddhe siddhiḥ tena anumā tridhā anyathā kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api pāka ādau kṛti sādhya tvam katham avagamyeta kiñca tava api iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt katham vṛṣṭi ādau= icchā siddhatvasya icchā virodhi tvāt anāgatasya jñātum aśakyatvāt atas eva siddha asiddha viṣaya tva nirāsena sukha ādi jñānāt phale api na icchā iti na vṛṣṭyādāviṣṭa sādhana tā api na ca vṛṣṭi ādi sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt vṛṣṭi ādau= icchā icchāyāḥ siddha asiddha vṛṣṭi ādi tad phala viṣaya tva vikalpa grāsāt 
TC_12.19^3	 atha sāmānya lakṣaṇa pratyāsattyā vṛṣṭi ādi tvena sukha ādi tvena ca siddha asiddha vṛṣṭi ādi tad phala viṣaya kam jñānam utpannam tena siddham virodhinam tyaktva asiddha viṣaya icchā utpadyate yadi ca sāmānya lakṣaṇā na asti tadā yena rūpeṇa iṣṭa sā dhana tva grahaḥ tena rūpeṇa jñāte siddhe vā icchā utpadyate anvaya vyatirekābhyām tādṛśa jñānasya tādṛśa icchā janaka tva avadhāraṇāt sukha icchāyām api ekam iti ced tarhi mama api pāka tvāt chedena kṛti sādhya tā jñānāt anāgate cikīrṣā tat ca jñānam sakala pāka viṣayam sannikṛṣṭa pāka viṣayam vā iti anyat etat bālasya vyāpti ādi a graheṇa ādyā pravṛttiḥ jīvana adṛṣṭa udbodhita janma antara saṃskāra janyāt stana pānam kāryam iti smaraṇāt tava api iṣṭa sādhana tā smaraṇāt tatra pravṛttiḥ ananya gatika tvāt 
TC_12.19^4	 na ca janma antare api paryanuyogaḥ janma dhārāyāḥ anādi tvāt pratyakṣa anumāna mūlaka tvāt ca na andha paramparā vastutas tu śuṣka kaṇṭha tayā bālaḥ duḥkham anubhavan virodhitayā sukham smarati tatas sukha tva jñānāt sukha vṛtti kārya tvam sukha vṛtti tayā antaraṅga tvāt na tu stana pānam iṣṭa sādhanam iti smaraṇam sukha āvṛtti tvena vahiḥ aṅga tvāt sukha kārya tvañca stana pānam api viṣayaḥ tena stana pāne kāryatva jñānāt eva pravṛttiḥ iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya tadānīm sa āmāgṣa bhāvāt evañca ādya pravṛttau kāryatva jñānam prayojakam kptam iti agre api tat eva pravartakam kpta tvāt 
TC_12.20	 navīnā astu mama idam kṛti sādhyam iti jñānam na pravartakam anāgata viṣaye pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ asambhavāt kintu yādṛśasya puruṣasya kṛti sādhyam yat dṛṣṭam tādṛśa tvam ātmanaḥ pratisandhāya tatra pravartate tathā hi odana kāmasya tad sādhana tā jñānavataḥ ca taṇḍula ādi upakaraṇavataḥ pākaḥ kṛti sādhyaḥ aham api ca tādṛśaḥ iti jñānāt pāke pravartate evañca anya kṛta pāke kṛti sādhya tā jñānam ātmanaḥ pāke kṛti sādhya tva prayojaka viśeṣaṇa vat tva jñānañca prapartakam anyatra api pravṛttiḥ evam eva iti anāditā eva atas eva sañcāta bādhaḥ caitya vandane viṣaya bhakṣaṇe ca na pravartate iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānavataḥ hi tat kṛti sādhyam na ca sañjāta bādhaḥ tatra iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānavān evam tṛpti icchāvataḥ api bhojanam kṛti sādhyam tṛptaḥ ca na tṛpti icchāvat tvam ātmani aveti iti na bhojane pravartate 
TC_12.21–12.22	 ati navīnāḥ tu yādṛśasya ityādau avigīta tvam tad kṛtau viśeṣaṇam āhuḥ sañjāta bādhaḥ tu viṣa bhakṣaṇam caitya vandanañca vigīta kṛtita adhya tvena eva jānāti iti tatra na pravartate pravṛtti viṣayaḥ ca sāmānyatas kāla asambhinnaḥ pāka ādiḥ jñāyate pravṛtti mahimnā ca anāgata pāka siddhiḥ cikīrṣā ca kāla asambhinna viṣayā na tu bhāvinam kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti ākārā eva iti 
TC_13.1^1	 atra ucyate viṣa bhakṣaṇa ādi vyāvṛttam kṛti sādhya tva jñāne iṣṭa sādhana tvam viṣaya tayā avacchedakam lāghavāt na tu sva viśeṣaṇa vat tā pratisandhāna janya tvam gauravāt na ca siddhāsiddha avasthayoḥ sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ virodhaḥ nirviśeṣitayoḥ tayoḥ avirodhāt pākaḥ asiddhaḥ sādhyaḥ siddhaḥ sādhanañca iti unubhavāt tadā sādhya tvam hi tadā sādhana tvasya virodhi niyamataḥ tena eva tasya pratikṣepeṇa saha anavasthāna niyamāt na tu sādhana tvasya anyadā sādhana tvasya vā tayoḥ apratikṣepāt anyadā sādhana tve api sādhana tvam asti eva sāmānya abhāve viśeṣa abhāva prasaṅgāt 
TC_13.1^2	 evantadāḥ asiddha tvasya tadā siddha tvam virodhi niyamataḥ tasya eva pratikṣepāt na tu siddha tva mātram anyat api tatra siddha tva abhāva prasaṅgāt nirviśeṣitayoḥ virodhe ca siddha tvayoḥ ca anyataradeva pāka ādau syāt na tu samaya bhede api ubhayam na ca tadā kṛti sādhya tve sati tadā iṣṭa sādhana tva jñānam pravartakam atas eva vājapeyena yajeta iti atra yāgasya karaṇa avasthāyām siddha tvena na vājapeyasya sādhya tā ekadā tayoḥ virodhāt iti karma nāmadheya tvam na tu karaṇasya siddha tvena sādhya tva virodhaḥ yoga svarūpe tayoḥ sattvāt 
TC_13.2^1	 atha viruddhayoḥ avacśebhedam ādayaḥ ekatra pratītiḥ syāt na ca kṛti sādhya tva iṣṭa sādhana tvayoḥ samaya bhedam ādaya ekatra pratītiḥ asti tathā liṅga abhāvāt iti ced na sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ avirodhasya ukta tvāt evam siddha tva asiddha tvayoḥ bhāva abhāva rūpa tve api na virodhaḥ eka dharmi ga tvena māna siddha tvāt tasmāt saṃyoga tadabhāvayoḥ iva yena prakāreṇa yayoḥ virodhaḥ tena tayoḥ eka dharmi gata tvam na pratīyate na tu rūpa antareṇa api iti api ca yadi sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ virodhaḥ tadā tava api iṣṭa sādhana tvena kārya sādhana tvena vā kārya tvam na anumīyate hetu sādhyayoḥ virodhena sāmāna adhikaraṇya abhāvena vyāpti asiddheḥ pakṣe sādhya sādhanayoḥ anyatara sattve bādhā asidhyoḥ anyatara prasaṅgāt ca 
TC_13.2^2	 na ca vācyam idānīm mad kṛti sādhya tvam sādhyam agre mad iṣṭa sādhana tvam hetuḥ daiva ādi anadhīna tve sati yat agre madiṣṭa asā dhanam tat idānīm mad kṛti sādhyam iti vyāptiḥ tathā ca samaya bhedam ādāya sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ avagamaḥ iti idānīm agrima padārthayoḥ nānā tvāt anugata rūpa abhāvena vyāpteḥ agrahāt pāka nyāyena anyatra api tad tad samaya antar bhāvena sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ apratītiḥ pratītau vā mama api idānīm kṛti sādhya tve sati agre iṣṭa sādhanam iti jñānam pravartakam astu na ca pāke sādhya iṣṭaka tvena kṛti sādhya tvam anumeyam asiddha avasthāvataḥ hi pāka ādiṣṭa anutpatteḥ pākasya siddhatvam avagamya tad sādhya tvam iṣṭasya avagantavyam asiddha tvañcau= agamya kṛti sādhya tvam iti siddha tva asiddha tvayoḥ virodhaḥ atra api durvāraḥ api ca sva viśeṣaṇa dhī janya kārya tā jñāna abhāvāt sukhe katham cikīrṣā na hi kṛti sādhya tā jñāna mātrāt sā sañjāta bādhasya viṣa bhakṣaṇa ādau cikīrṣā prasaṅgāt 
TC_13.2^3	 atha upāya cikīrṣāyām tad kāraṇam icchā karaṇa sukha tva jñāne kṛti sādhya tvam yadā viṣayaḥ tadā sukhe cikīrṣā no ced icchā mātram iti dvayam eva cikīrṣā hetuḥ iti ced tarhi icchā hetu jñāne yadā kṛti sādhya tvam bhāsate tāda cikīrṣā no ced icchā mātram iti eva sukha tad upāya cikīrṣā kāraṇam astu lāghavāt sukha tva jñāna vat iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya api icchā kāraṇa tvāt atas eva pāke iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāne kṛti sādhya tvam viṣayaḥ iti tatra cikīrṣā na tu vṛṣṭi ādi jñāne tad viṣaya tvam iti icchā mātram sukha cikīrṣāyām icchā kāraṇa jñāne kṛti sādhya tā viṣayake cikīrṣā janakatva avadhāraṇāt anyathā tatra cikīrṣā anutpatteḥ vastu tas tu upāya cikīrṣā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna sādhyāḥ upāya icchā tvāt vṛṣṭī i= chāvat na ca bhoga cikīrṣā vat tena vinā api syāt iti aprayoñjaka tvam upāya icchāyāḥ tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt vṛṣṭeḥ ca svatas asundara tvena icchā anutpatteḥ anugata upāya icchāyām anugatasya prayojaka tve sambhavati bādhakam vinā tyāga ayogāt ca 
TC_13.2^4–13.3	 na ca cikīrṣā anya tve sati upāya icchātvam icchā tvam vā tad janya tve prayojakam gauravāt sukha icchāyām tad abhāvāt ca evañcopāya cikīrṣāyām iṣṭa sādhana tva jñāne dhruve ati prasaṅga vāraṇa artham kṛti sādhya tva nirvāha arthañca kṛti sādhya tvam api viṣaya tayā avacchedakam astu na tu tad vihāya tanmātram kpta kāraṇam vinā kārya anupapatteḥ atas eva stana pāna pravṛttau= api upāya it chā kāraṇa tvena gṛhītasya iṣṭa sādhana tva jñānasya api kalpanam dṛṣṭa anurodhi tvāt kalpanāyāḥ nanu sādhana tvam icchā virodhi tasya siddha dharma tvāt vṛṣṭi ādau tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt iccha iti ced na nirviśeṣitayoḥ siddha tva asiddha tvayoḥ avirodhena icchā sādhana tvayoḥ avirodhāt tadā asiddha tvam tadā siddhatvañca na icchā sādhana tvayoḥ prayojakam iti tathā na jñāyate eva yat tu tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt vṛṣṭi ādau= icchā iti tad tuccham asiddha avasthāt vṛṣṭi ādeḥ iṣeṭa an utpatteḥ tasya avaśyam siddha tvam avagantavyam icchā anurodhi tvāt ca asiddha tvam iti 
TC_13.4^1	 tatra api virodhaḥ eva vṛṣṭau satyām iṣṭam tayā vinā na iti anvaya vyatireka grahasya vṛṣṭi siddha tvam ādāya vṛṣṭi nirūpita iṣṭa sādhyaka tva grāhaka tvāt kiñca cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhyam maṇḍalīkaraṇam iti artha pratipādakam amaṇḍalīm kuryāt iti vākyam pramāṇam syāt viṣaya ābādhāt etena navīna matam api apāstam parasya hi kṛti sādhya tva odana kāma nāvat tva iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānānām jñānam tathā ātmana odana kāmān āvat tevaṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya jñānam na pravṛtti kāraṇam gauravāt kintu mad kṛti sādhya tve sati mad iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam eva lāghavāt yathā ca sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ avirodhaḥ anāgatasya pāka ādeḥ kṛti sādhya tva jñānañca tathā upapāditam eva kiñca para kṛti sādhya tvam ajñātvā api sva kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt sva kalpita lipya ādau yauvane kāma udrekāt sambhoga ādau pravṛtteḥ ca tat eva pravartakam 
TC_13.4^2	 vastutas tu siddha viṣaya ka kṛti sādhya ta ajñānāt katham kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchā siddhe icchā virahāt asiddhasya ajñānāt atha siddha viṣayāt eva kṛti sādhya tā jñānāt asiddha viṣayā kṛti sādhya tvena icchā jñāyate icchāyā asiddha viṣaya tva svabhāva tvāt eka prakāraka tvena jñāna cikīrṣayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na tu eka viṣaya tve sati gauravāt icchāyāḥ anāgata viṣaya tvāt tasya ca ajñānāt tathā tva darśanāt sukha ādi icchāyām api evam iti ced na asiddha viṣaya icchā anu rodhena anāgata jñāna upāyasya darśita tvāt astu ca evam tathā api kṛti sādhya tā jñāne iṣṭa sādhana tvam eva vyāvartakam astu sva parakīya iṣṭa sā adhana tā jñāna phala kāmanā jñāna apekṣayā laghu tvāt iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna jñānasya phala kāmanā jñānasya ca hetu tve māna abhāvāt ca 
TC_13.5^1	 navyāḥ tu sva kṛti sādhya ta ajñānam eva pravartakam tena sva kṛtya sādhye vṛṣṭi ādau kārīḥ yāñca kṛṣīvalasya na pravṛttiḥ na ca san jāta bādhasya viṣa bhakṣaṇe pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ sva kṛti sādhya ta ajñāna viṣaye iṣṭa tvasya svarūpa satas pravṛttau sahakāri tvāt na ca san jāta bādhasya viṣa bhakṣaṇāt ā= icchā asti iṣṭa sādhana tvena ajñānāt atīta bhojane api atas eva na pravartate tṛpteḥ siddha tayā icchā viraheṇa bhojane tad upādhika iṣṭa tva abhāvāt atīta tṛptau= icchā na asti iti tad sādhane api iṣṭa tva abhāvāt eva na pravṛttiḥ na ca evam pāke na pravarteta tasya svarasa taiṣṭa tva abhāvāt iti vācyam 
TC_13.5^2	 iṣṭa sādhana tva jñānena tasya api iṣṭa tvāt hanta evam prāthamika tvāt iṣṭa tva artham avaśya apekṣaṇīya tvāt ca kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam eva cikīrṣā kāraṇam astu iti ced na iṣṭa asādhana tva abhāve api bhoge cikīrṣā sattvāt tasyām sva kṛti sādhana tva abhāve api bhoge cikīrṣā sattvāt tasyām sva kṛti sādhya tva jñāne sati iṣṭa tvam eva kāraṇam na tu iṣṭa sādhana tvam vyabhicārāt pāka ādau tad anvaya vyatireka avapīṣṭa tva upakṣāṇau evam bhoge api pravarteta iti ced na iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api mukti rūpa iṣṭa sādhane sukhe pravarteta iti tulyam sukhe cikīrṣā bhavati eva kṛtiḥ tu na bhavati kṛteḥ 
TC_13.6^1	 siddha vṛtti asiddha kriyā viṣaya tva niyamāt iti ced tulyam tasmāt sva kṛti sādhya tvam vidhiḥ iṣṭa tvam sahakārī iti mā evam iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya upāya icchāyām hetu tva avadhāraṇāt tasyāḥ tad janya tva niyamāt i= chāyāḥ sva viṣaya icchā anutpādaka tva niyamāt ca nanu siddhaudanaḥ kutas pāke na pravartate odana mātrasya siddha tvena iṣṭatva abhāvāt atas eva atīta bhojana ādau na pravartate atīta tṛṣṇā ādau= icchā virahāt nanu sāmudraka vikhyāte bhāvi yauvana rojye bhoga sādhane sva kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tva jñānāt kutas na pravartate bhāvi rājyasya asiddha tvāt pravatteḥ siddha viṣaya tva niyamāt rājya upāya aparicayāt ca tad paricaye ca pravartate eva devatā ārādhana ādau= iti ced na siddhe cikīrṣā viraheṇa yāga ādau= api apravṛtti prasaṅgāt devatā ārādhana ādeḥ api asiddha tve na tatra api apravṛtti prasaṅgāt ca kiñca rājya upayāparicaye tatra mā pravarttiṣṭa sva kṛti sādhyeṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāne rājye pravṛtti prasaṅge kim āyātam 
TC_13.6^2	 na hi kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāne api tad upāya jñānam tatra pravartakam gauravāt bhinna viṣaya tvāt ca iti ced mā evam yauvane hi yāvat pravartate eva rājye bālye tu rājya upāyam akṛtvā mad kṛtya idānīm rājyam na siddhyati iti sva kṛtya sādhyata ajñānāt eva na pravartate yathā taṇḍulam vinā pāke sva kṛti asādhyatā jñānāt rājya upāye tu sva kṛti sādhyeṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāte devatā ārādhana ādau pravartate eva atas eva vrīhi avaghātam akṛtvā puroḍāśaḥ tam akṛtvā yāgaḥ tam akṛtvā apavūrvam sādhayitum na śakyate iti kramaśas avaghāta ādau pravartate na yugapad siddha vṛtti asiddha kriyā viṣaya aviṣaya svabhāva tvāt pravṛtteḥ yāga anantarañca na apūrve pravartate 
TC_13.6^3	 kṛti antaram vinā eva yāga kṛtitaḥ tad sambhavāt iṣṭa sādhane ceṣṭā utpattinā antarīyaka duḥkha ājanaka tvam viśeṣaṇam na tu tad jñāna abhāvaḥ kāraṇam kintu tat eva viṣaya tayā kāraṇa tāvacchedakam lāghavāt tena madhu viṣa sampṛkta anna bhojane na pravṛttiḥ pareṇa api pravṛtti pūrvam liṅga viśeṣaṇa tvena anyathā vā tad jñāna viniyoga svīkārāt evañca alpa āyāsa sādhya ādiṣṭa utpatti sambhave bahu āyāsa sādhye na pravṛttiḥ atas eva śruta svarga phalaka tve api bahu vitta vyayāsa sādhye jyotiṣṭoma ādau phala bhūmā kalpane anyathā alpa āyāsa asadhyāt eva svarga siddhi sambhave tatra apravṛttau ananuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇam aprāmāṇyam tad vidheḥ syāt 
TC_13.7^1	 balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi tvañca na viśeṣaṇam bahu vitta vyaya āyāsa sādhya bahutara duḥkhasya api abalavat tvam kvacid alpa duḥkhasya api balavat tvam tasya api ukta atiriktasya ananugamāt āstikasya niṣiddha tvena jñāte api pravṛttiḥ rāga dveṣayoḥ utkaṭa tvena naraka sādhana tva jñāna tirodhānāt nanu na kalañjam bhakṣayet iti atra vidhi artha niṣedha anupapattiḥ tad bhakṣaṇasya tṛpti rūpa iṣṭa sādhana tvāt 
TC_13.7^2	 na ca asura avidyā ādi vat paryudāsa lakṣaṇayā virodhi aniṣṭa sādhana tva bodhanam nañaḥ asamasta tvāt kriyā saṅgata tvena pratiṣadha vācaka tva vyutpatteḥ ca iti ced na viśeṣyavati viśiṣṭa niṣedhasya sa viśeṣaṇe hi iti nyāyena viśeṣaṇa niṣedha paryavamāyitayā kalañja bhakṣaṇam iṣṭa utpattinā antarīyaka duḥkha atirikta duḥkha sādhanam iti na kalañjam bhakṣayet iti anena bodhanāt iṣṭa sādhana tā vācakasya siddheḥ sāmānyatas niṣedha anupapatteḥ balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi iṣṭa sādhana tva viśeṣa niṣedha tātparyam tathā ca aśakya viśeṣa niṣedha paratvam nañaḥ iti kaścid tat na yathā hi ayogya tayā sa= chidram vihāya ghaṭa tvena tad itara anvayaḥ na tu chidra itara tvena yugapad vṛtti dvaya virodhāt tathā atra api balavat aniṣṭa an anubandhi tvena anupasthitau katham tat niṣedhaḥ 
TC_13.7^3	 śyenena abhicaran yajeta iti atra katham vidhi pravṛttiḥ hiṃsāyāḥ balavat aniṣṭa anubandhi tvāt iti ced tatra kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhantvam eva yogyatayā anveti na tu balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi tvam api ayogya tvāt nindā artha vādena prāyaścitta upadeśena ca hiṃsāyāḥ balavat aniṣṭa anubandhi tva avagamāt atas eva vihite apiśyene vigānāt na tātvika pravṛttiḥ rāga dveṣayoḥ utkaṭa tvena aniṣṭa anubandhi aṃśasya tiraskārāt kasyacid pravṛttiḥ iti eke anye tu abhicārasya vairi badha phalaka tvena śruta tvāt badha sādhana tvena śyenaḥ vidhīyate na tu badha sādhya naraka sādhana tvena narakasya phala tvena aśruteḥ na ca janaka janakasya janakatva niyamaḥ kumbhakāra pitṛ paramparāyāḥ kumbha janakatva āpatteḥ vidhinā eva śyenasya balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi tva bodhanāt ca na ca śyenasya balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi tva bodhanāt ca na ca śyenasya naraka ahetu tve apekṣita vairi badha hetu tve vā avigānena pravṛttiḥ syāt iti vācyam śyenāt badho badhāt ca avaśyam narakaḥ iti pratisandhānena vigānāt 
TC_13.8^1	 nanu śyenaḥ maraṇa phalaka vyāpāra tvena hiṃsā sā ca naraka janikā iti ced na na hi sākṣāt paramparā sā dhāraṇa maraṇa phala kavyāpāraḥ hiṃsā kūpa ādau vinaṣṭe gavi tad karttuḥ go badha kaṛttutva āpatteḥ badhyasya api hantuḥ mṛtyu utpādana dvāreṇa ātma hantṛ tva prasaṅgāt ca na hi anutpādita manyuḥ kaścid kam api vyāpādayati kintu anuniṣpādi maraṇa phala kaḥ vyāpāraḥ hiṃsā yat anantaram maraṇam bhavati eva na ca śyenaḥ tathā kintu khaṅga hanana ādikam eva atha maraṇān uddeśena kṣipta nārācāt hata brāhyaṇe ca hiṃsā na syāt kiñca hinasti dhātu arthe avacchedakam phalam avyavahitam eva maraṇam avyavahita phalakasya eva vyāpārasya dhātu vācya tvāt anyathā paramparayā vilkipti phalaka anna kāma iṣṭa taṇḍula kraya ādau= api pacati iti prasaṅgāt 
TC_13.8^2	 evam khaṅga abhighāta anantaram yatra vilambena maraṇam vraṇa pāka paramparayā vai anne viṣa prayogeṇa vā tatra hantṛ tvam prāyaścitta ādi ca na syāt iti ced na prāyaścitta tulya tā artham hi tatra hantṛvya deśaḥ gauṇaḥ vinigama kañca lāghavam eva vastutas tu maraṇa uddeśena kṛtaḥ adṛṣṭāt vārākaḥ tad anukūla vyāpāraḥ hiṃsā kūpa ādau vinaṣṭe gavi tad kartuḥ go badha ka ṛtu tva āpatteḥ badhyasya api hantuḥ mutyu utpādana dvāreṇa ātma hantṛ tva prasaṅgāt ca na hi anutpādita manyuḥ kaścid kam api vyāpādayati kintu anuniṣpādi maraṇa phala kovyāparaḥ hiṃsā yad anantaram maraṇam bhavati eva na ca śyenaḥ tathā kintu khaṅga hanana ādikam eva atha maraṇa ānukūlī a vyāpāraḥ maraṇa uddaśena anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ hiṃsā śyenaḥ ca tathā kūpa ādau ca na maraṇa uddeśena anuṣṭhīyamāna tvam iti ced naḥ evam sati gauravāt maraṇān uddeśena kṣipta nārācāt hata brāhmaṇe ca hiṃsā na syāt 
TC_13.9^1	 kiñca hinasti dhātu arthe avacchedakam phalam avyavahitam eva maraṇam avyavahita phalakasya eva vyāpārasya dhātu vācya tvāt anyathā paramparayā viklitti phalaka anna kāma iṣṭa taṇḍula kraya ādau= api pacati iti prasaṅgāt evam khaṅga abhighāta anantaram yatra vilambena maraṇam vraṇa pāka paramparayā vai anne viṣa prayogeṇa vā tatra hantṛ tvam prāyaścitta ādi ca na syāt iti ced prāyaścitta tulya tā artham hi tatra hantṛ vyapadeśaḥ gauṇaḥ vinigama kañca lāghavam eva vastutas tu maraṇa uddeśena kṛtaḥ adṛṣṭāt vārakaḥ tad anukūlya vyāpāraḥ hiṃsā śyenaḥ ca adṛṣṭa dvārakaḥ tanu kūlya vyāpāraḥ hiṃsā śyenaḥ ca adṛṣṭa dvārā maraṇa sādhanam atas na hiṃsā 
TC_13.9^2–13.10	 yadi ca adṛṣṭa dvārā api maraṇa sādhanam hiṃsā syāt tadā saptamī taila abhyaṅgasya adṛṣṭa dvārā iṣṭa bhārya vināśa hetu tvāt abhyaṅga kartu hiṃsaka tva āpattiḥ atas eva kūpa ādau gomaraṇe api na badha kartu tvam tat kartuḥ gala lagna anna maraṇe na bhoktuḥ na vā pariveṣayituḥ ātma hantṛ tvam brahma hantṛ tvam vā vraṇa pāka paramparayā vilambena viṣa prayogeṇa ca hantṛ tvam mukhyam eva na tu anuniṣpādi maraṇa phalaka tvam gala lagna anna maraṇe sva hantṛ tva āpatteḥ anya uddaśena kṣipta nārācena hate brāhmaṇe brahma hantṛ tvam syāt iti ced na iṣṭa āpatteḥ vyapadeśaḥ tu gauṇaḥ prayoga ulakṣaṇayā api samarthayitum śakyate tat pakṣe ati prasaṅgaḥ vārayitum na śakyate iti idam eva vinigamakam atas eva atad uddeśena kṛte api niṣiddhe prāyaścitta arddham uktam 
TC_13.11	 apare tu anabhisaṃhita nara antara vyāpāram advārīkṛtya maraṇa sādhanam hiṃsā khaṅga kārasya anabhisaṃhita nara antara vyāpāra dvārā maraṇa sādhana tvam tasya hi nara antara vyāpāra dvārāḥ maraṇa sādhana tvam tasya hi nara antara vyāpāraḥ nābhisaṃhitaḥ kintu dhana lābhaḥ iti khaṅga kāraḥ na ghātakaḥ viṣasya anne prakṣepeṇa nara antara vyāpāraḥ bhojanam eva abhisaṃhitaḥ anena idam bhoktavyam iti abhisandhāya viṣa prayogāt iti hisā eva anne viṣa prayogaḥ iti tat na gala lagna kavalāt i atra maraṇam tatra pariveṣa yituḥ ghātaka tā āpātāt anena idam bhoktavyam iti abhisandhāya parivaṣaṇāt bhoktuḥ ātma hantṛ tva āpatteḥ ca anabhisaṃhita nara antara vyāpāram advārīkṛtya maraṇa anukūlānnaṃbhakṣaṇa anuṣṭhānāt atas eva avyavahita prāṇa viyoga phalakaḥ vyāpāraḥ hiṃsā vraṇa pāka paramparā mṛte tu hantṛ tvam vyāpārasya avyavadhāyaka tvāt iti nirastam 
TC_13.12^1	 syāt etat na iṣṭa sādhana tā vidhiḥ nitye sandhyā upāsana ādau phala abhāvāt atha na asti eva tat nityam yatra artha vāda ādikam vidhi vākye vā na phalam śrutam asti sandhyām upāsate ye tu satatam śaṃsita vratāḥ vidhūta pāpāḥ te yānti brahma lokam sanātanam iti ādi artha vādāt dadyāt aharahar śrāddham pitṛbhyaḥ prītim āvahan ityādi vidhi vākya śravaṇāt ca kṛtvā acintayā tu ucyate yatra na phala śrutiḥ tatra viśvajinna yāyāt svargaḥ phalam iti ced na kāmanā upādhi kārya tvena yāga vat nitya tā bhaṅga prasaṅgāt aharahar śrutyā hi tad kāla jīvi mātra kṛti sādhyam sandhyā vandanam avagatam hi kāmanā upādhi kārya tve ca yadā phala kāmanā na asti tadā tad samayaḥ eva tad kartavyatā na syāt na hi tad kāle phala kāmanā vaśyambhāvaḥ pramāṇa bhāvāt 
TC_13.12^2	 kiñca prathama pravṛtta itara nirapekṣā harahar śrutyā jīvi mātrasya adhikāraḥ avagataḥ tathā ca tad sa apekṣa caram apravṛtti artha vāda upanīta phala kāmasya na tatra adhikāraḥ prathama pravṛtta aharahar śruti virodhāt nitye phala śruteḥ artha vādasya ca stutau tātparyam atas eva pratyavāya parihāraḥ api na phalam tad kāmanā upādhi kārya tve nitya tā kṣateḥ 
TC_13.12^3	 kiñca nitye kartavya tā bodhanāt prāk na pratyavāye pramāṇam asti vidheḥ kartavya tvam avagamya kartavyā karaṇe pratyavāya kalpanam yena anyonya āśrayaḥ kintu nindā artha vādena prāyaścitta upadeśena ca upāsanasya prakṛti arthasya tāvat vyāpāra svarūpasya abhāvaḥ pratyavāya hetuḥ avagataḥ tathā ca sandhyā upāsana abhāvaḥ pratyavāya dvārāḥ duḥkha sādhanam tad abhāvaḥ sandhyā upāsanam duḥkha sādhana abhava tvena phalam prāyaścitte pāpa dhvaṃsa vat iti tad sādhana tvena kṛtiḥ bodhyate vidhinā na ca evam pratyavāya parihāraḥ eva phalam astu iti vācyam parihārasya prāc abhāva rūpa tvena anāditayā asādhya tvāt 
TC_13.12^4	 na ca upāsana ākaraṇam pratyavāya hetuḥ na upāsana abhāvaḥ tathā ca duḥkha sādhana abhāva tvena kṛtiriṣṭāḥ na tu upāsanam iti vācyam nindā artha vādasya ubhayatra sattvena ubhayasya api tathā tvāt iti tat naḥ evam api kāmya tve nitya tā kṣati prasaṅgāt kiñca akurvan vihitam karma ityādinā na upāste yaḥ ca paścimām ityādinā ca karaṇa abhāvasya eva pratyavāya hetu tvam bodhyate na tu tad viṣaya abhāvasya anyathā akartuḥ pratyavāyaḥ na anyasya iti katham syāt viṣaya abhāvasya sādharaṇyāt vastutas tu kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam pravartaka tvena nirvyūḍham na ca kṛtau kṛti sādhya tvam asti iti atas na kiñcid etat 
TC_13.13	 navyāḥ tu nitya apūrva prāgabhāvaḥ durita dvārā duḥkha sādhanam tad abhāvaḥ a pūrvam duḥkha sādhana abhāva tvena iṣṭam tad sādhana tvena kṛti sādhya tvena ca sandhyā upāsanam vidhīyate iti tat na nindā artha vāda ādinā sandhyā upāsana abhāvaḥ tad akaraṇam vā pratyavāya hetuḥ avagataḥ na tu apūrvā bhāvaḥ prathamam pramāṇa abhāvena tad anupasthiteḥ vidheḥ iṣṭa sādhana tva bodhaka tvāt pariśeṣeṇa apūrvam iṣṭam kalpyate iti ced tarhi viśvajit nayāyena svargaḥ eva phalam kalpyatām kāmya tvasya tvayā api svīkārāt kiñca vidhi pravṛttau= apūrva jñānam apūrva jñāne ca vidhi pravṛttiḥ iti anyonya āśrayaḥ 
TC_13.14	 yāvat nitya naimittika nirvāhasya tad tad āśrayam avihita karmaṇām samyak paripālanasya ca brahma loka avāptiḥ phalam śrūyate tathā ca nityasya saphala tvam iti kecid tat na tasya vidheḥ nitya vidhim upajīvya pravṛttiḥ tasya ca phala abhāvena prathamam mūka tvāt anyathā paraspara sāpekṣa tvena anyonya āśrayaḥ tasmāt kārya tā eva vidhiḥ nanu nitye vedāt kārya tā jñāne api prayojana jñānam vinā katham pravṛttiḥ na hi prayojanam uddiśya mandaḥ api pravartate iti ced na nitye phala bādhena pravṛtti mātre prayojana jñānasya aprayojaka tvāt kāmye api prayojana jñānam na sākṣāt pravartakam upāya viṣaya tvāt prayojane apravṛtteḥ ca kintu iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna dvārā kārya tā jñāne upakṣīṇam eva katham ayam niścayaḥ nitye iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna asambhavāt kārya tā ajñānasya vedāt api sambhavāt nanu niṣphale duḥkha eka phale vā prekṣāvatām katham pravṛttiḥ veda adhīna kārya tā jñāna sattvāt saphala pravṛttau= api tasya eva tantra tvāt yat tu laukike niṣphale duḥkha eka phale vā na pravartate tat iṣṭa sādhana tā āliṅgakasya 
TC_13.15^1	 kārya tā ajñānasya veda adhīnasya vā abhāvāt na ca duḥkha eka phala tva jñānam pravṛtti pratibandhakam sati kārya tā jñāne tasya pratibandhaka tva adarśanāt atha vā kāmye liṅgaḥ apūrva vācatvāt nitye api liṅga upāsana ādi viṣaya kamapūrvam bodhyate tat ca niṣphalam api stataḥ eva sukha vat prayojanam nityam abhyarthyam ānañca iti ucyate 
TC_13.15^2	 sarvatra nitye phala śravaṇa jīvi phala kāmasya sambalita adhikāraḥ yathā uparāge naimittikam snāna śrāddha ādi phala śruteḥ kāmyam akaraṇe prāyaścitta ādi śruteḥ ca niyata kartavya tākam yathā vā ṣoḍaśa śrāddhasya preta tva vimukti kāmanā śruteḥ preta tva vimukti hetu ṣoḍaśa śrāddhe saṅkalpam vidhāya mahājanānām ācārāt kāmya tvam nindā artha vādena akaraṇe pratyavāya śruteḥ avaśya kartavya tvam tathā sandhyā upāsanam api phala śruteḥ kāmyam akaraṇe naraka śruteḥ prāyaścitta upadeśāt ca niyata kartavya tāka tvam tat akaraṇe prāyaścitta anupadeśāt na ca nitye phala kāmanāyāḥ asambhavaḥ tri kāla kamyaḥ tava pāṭha vat nitye phala kāmanā sambhavāt yat tu prathama pravṛttā aharahar śrutyā tad kāla jīvi mātrasya adhikāra bodhanāt na phala kāmasya adhikāraḥ iti tat na aharahar śruti artha vādayoḥ prathama gṛhīta eka vākyatā balena tad kāla jīvi phala anvayam vinā eka vākyata aṅgāt 
TC_13.15^3	 na ca artha vādasya stuti paratvāt na eka vākyatā bādhakam vinā sva artha parityāgāt vidhivā vākya upasthite phale vidhi vākya stha phalam ādāya eva aharahar śrutyā kārya tā bodhanāt nanu evam tad kāla jīvi kāminaḥ adhikāre yadā phala kāmanā virahaḥ tadā aśuceḥ iva adhikāra abhāvāt niyata kartavyatā na syāt adhikṛta akaraṇe pratyavāyaḥ na tu akaraṇa mātraḥ iti ced na naimittike api tad kāle kasyacid kāmanā virahiṇaḥ aniyata kartavyatā āpatteḥ atha apavāda abhāvena autsikī phala kāmanā asti eva phala jñānasya sva viṣayaka icchā janaka svabhāvāt yasya tu mumukṣa apavādena phala antare kāmanā na asti tasya akaraṇe api na pratyavāyaḥ iti na tat niyata kartavya tāka tvam naimittike tathā nitye api mumukṣayā phala kāmanā bādhena akaraṇe api na pratyavāyaḥ iti tulyam 
TC_13.15^4	 kiñca arthavāda upasthita phala upādhi kartavya tve avagate akurvan vihitam karma ityādi vākyāt śauce sati sandhyau= andhākaraṇe nindā artha vādena ca naraka śruteḥ prāyaścitta upadeśāt ca pratyavāyaḥ kalpyate tad phala kāmanā virahe api pratyavāya parihāra artham niyamataḥ pravartate vidhi pravṛtti anantaram pratyavāyasya prāmāṇika tvāt akaraṇa unmukhasya karaṇena pratyavāya pragābhāvasya sādhya tvāt naimittike phala upādhi kartavya tve kāmanā virahe api niyata kartavya tāvat 
TC_13.16^1	 yat tu niṣphale api nitye veda ādīn akārya tā jñānāt pravartate iti tat na duḥkha eka phala tvena jñāyamāne prekṣāvatām kṛteḥ anutpāda niyamāt ayogya tayā nitye kṛti sādhya tvasya bodhayitum aśakyatvāt atas eva sandhyā upāsana phalam api kriyate veda bodhita kartavya tāka tvāt iti āśaṅkya guru matam etat na guroḥ matam iti abhiprāyeṇa upekṣitavān ācāryaḥ yat tu pāṇḍa apūrvam svatas eva prayojanam iti uktam tat api na evam tava api kāmya tve nitya tva hāni āpatteḥ kiñca sukham duḥkha abhāvaḥ ca mukhyam prayojanam tad sādhanañca gauṇam nitya apūrvantu prayojanam 
TC_13.16^2	 pravartaka vidhi anurodhena tat api pravartakam kalpyate iti ced na pravartanīyena lokena tasya prayojana tvena ajñānāt guruṇā nitya apūrvam prayojanam uktam iti ucyamāne api na ādaraḥ prekṣāvatām mukti svargau ca alaukikau= api sukha duḥkha abhāvasa jātīya tayā prayojane tasmāt evam vadan guruḥ api laghuḥ eva tat ayam saṅkṣepaḥ nitye duḥkha eka phala tvena pravṛtti anupapatteḥ phala upādhi kartavya tā tat ca phalam duḥkha sādhana abhāvaḥ pāṇḍa apūrvam vā iti tad icchā pravṛtti artham pratyaham upeyā tām vinā pravṛtti anupapatteḥ tathā ca artha vādikam vidhi vākya śru tañca phalam astu kṛtam anyena 
TC_13.16^3	 na ca kāmanā virahe niyata kartavyatā na syāt apūrva ādi icchā virahe api tulya tvāt pratyavāya parihāra artham niyamataḥ pravṛttiḥ tulyā eva yatra ca na phala śrutiḥ tatra viśvajit nayāyaḥ iti nanu idam iṣṭa sādhanam iti jñānāt etat sādhyam iṣṭam iti jñānāt ca pravṛtti darśanāt prathamasya eva pravartaka tve kim vinigamakam ucyate phala icchāyām sva viṣaya viśeṣyaka jñānasya hetu tvena kpta tvāt upāya cikīrṣā api bādhakam vinā tathā 
TC_13.16^4	 vastutas tu kṛti sādhya yāgasya sādhyaḥ iṣṭaḥ iti jñānasya pravartaka tve yajeta iti padāt prathamam kṛti sādhyaḥ yāgaḥ iti jñānam tatas kṛti sādhya yāgasya sādhyaḥ iṣṭaḥ iti jñānam viśeṣaṇa jñāna sādhya tvāt viśiṣṭa jñānasya iti jñāna dvayam tava mama tu yāgaḥ kṛti sādhyaḥ iṣṭa sādhanam iti ekam eva jñānam na ca kṛti sādhya tvam yāge bodhayitvā kṛti sādhya yāgasya sādhyaḥ iṣṭaḥ iti liṅgāḥ bodhayitum śakyam api eka sva artha anvayam apara padārthe bodhayitvā tad anvita apara sva artha anvaya bodhaka tvasya pade avyuptatteḥ yajipade ca kṛtyā saha yāga anvayam bodhayitvā tad anvita apara sva artha anvaya bodhaka tvasya pade avyutpatteḥ yajipade ca kṛtyā saha yāga anvayam bodhayitvā paryavasite punar sva artha anvaya bodhaka tve āvṛtti prasaṅgaḥ 
TC_13.17	 atha sādhyam iṣṭam yasya iti sādhya iṣṭaka tvam śakyam tathā ca bahuvrrīhi artha apekṣayā iṣṭasya sādhanam iti padi arthasya laghu tvāt tat eva śakyam kiñca tad sādhya tvam na niyamataḥ tat uttara sattvam daṇḍa sādhye ghaṭe vyabhicārāt na api tad avacchinna kṣaṇa uttarakṣaṇaḥ eva sattvam eva kāra vyavacchedya tad anuttara samayasya ākāśe aprasiddheḥ śabdasya 
TC_13.18^1	 tat asādhya tva āpatteḥ atas eva na tad abhāva vyāpaka abhāva pratiyāgi tvam rūpe rasa sādhya tva āpatteḥ ca na api tad avadhika uttara tva vyāpya samaya sambandhaḥ uttara tva vyāpya tvam hi uttara tva an adhikaraṇa kāla āvṛtti tvam tat ca ākāśe aprasiddham gurutarañcaḥ tasmāt tat sādhanaka tvam eva tad sādhya tvam evañca lāghavāt tad sādhana tva jñānam eva pravartakam na tu tad sādhanaka tva jñānam iti syāt etat iṣṭa tva jñānasya pravartaka tve tṛptaḥ api bhojane pravarteta manasā tṛpteḥ iṣṭa tva jñānāt atha svarūpasatī api phala icchā kāraṇam sā ca siddha tayā tṛptau na asti iti ced tarhi hantā evam āvaśyaka tvāt phala icchā eva kāraṇam na tu tat jñānam gauravāt 
TC_13.18^2	 kiñca icchā jñānasya kāraṇa tve icchā kāraṇam na syāt sva jñānena tad nāśāt icchā tad jñāna dhārā kalpane anavasthānāt api ca icchā viṣayaḥ sukham iti jñānam na mānasam sukhasya asiddha tayā tad viśeṣyaka sākṣātkārasya tad sannikarṣam vinā abhāvāt odana ādau= api iṣṭa tva jñānam na sambhavati manāsaḥ bahis asvātantrāt na api cakṣuḥ ādinā jñātaḥ kṛtaḥ iti vat iṣṭa tva jñānam tatra viśeṣya sannikarṣāt vastutas tu iṣṭasya viśiṣya sukha tva ādinā ajñāne yāga pākādāviṣṭa sādhana tā jñānepya pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ iṣṭasya apalpa adhika bhāvena nānā prakāra tvena ca viśiṣya anadhyavasāyāt 
TC_13.18^3	 na ca iṣṭa viṣaya tā avacchedaka sukha tva ādeḥ upalakṣaṇam iṣṭa tvam sukha duḥkha abhāva tad sādhaneṣu anugatasya upalakṣyasya abhāvena ananugamāt iti ucyate yatra icchā tad sādhana tā jñānam eva loka vedasādhāraṇam pravartakam teṣām sukha duḥkha abhāva tad sādhana tvena icchā viṣayāṇām ananugatānām api vastu sadicchā viṣaya tvam eva anugamakam evam yadā sukha ādau= icchā bhavati sva kṛti sādhya tve sati sukha ādi sādhanam iti jñānam tadā pāka ādau pravartate nanu evam pravartaka jñāna viṣasya nānā tvena tad śaktasya vidhi pratyayasya nānā artha tva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na sukha tva ādinā ananugatam iṣṭa tvena anugatam phalam prati sādhana tvasya yāga ādeḥ liṅga ādinā bodhanāt tathā ca phalānām anugama artham phala icchā śakyāḥ na tu icchā jñāna kāraṇa tvena 
TC_13.18^4–13.19	 atha evam sukha ādi sādhana tvena jñānam pravartakam tat na śakyam ananugamāt yat ca śakyam iṣṭa sādhana tvam tat jñānam na pravartakam iti vidheḥ pravartaka tā na syāt iti ced sākṣāt evam eva kintu iṣṭa sādhanam yāga eti liṅgāḥ bodhite iṣṭa ākāṅkṣāyām kāmya tvena śrutaḥ svargaḥ eva iṣṭa tvena avagamyate tad anantaram svarga kāma pada samabhivyāhārāt svarga sādhanam yāgaḥ iti jñānam pravartakam utpadyate evañca vidhi janya jñāna janyam jñānam pravartakam yat tu sarveṣām eva vidheḥ na sākṣāt pravartakam vidhi bodhakāt sva kṛti sādhya tva ādeḥ anavagamāt sva iṣṭa sādhanatvañca aham iṣṭa sādhana yāgakaḥ svarga kāma tvāt darśa vākya avagata svarga kāma vat iti anantaram arthāt pratīyate tat na yatra icchā tad sādhanam iti śābda jñānāt eva pravṛtti upapatteḥ tad pratītiḥ niṣphalāḥ 
TC_13.20	 anye tu sādhana tva mātram vidhi arthaḥ svarga ādi sādhana tāla ābhaḥ tu samabhivyāhārāt iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api tasya upajīvya tvāt tathā hi yajeta iti anena yāgaḥ kṛti sādhyaḥ sādhanañca iti bodhite sādhanasya sādhya ākāṅkṣāyām kāmanā viṣaya tvena śrutī asiddhaḥ svargaḥ eva sādhana ākāṅkṣaḥ sādhya tvena avagamyate upasthita tvāt na ca yāgasya sādhana ākāṅkṣā kṛti sādhya tvena eva upasthiteḥ atas eva viśva jit ādau svargaḥ eva sādhya tvena kalpyate iti iṣṭa sādhana tā vidhi pakṣe api tarati mṛtyum tarati brahmahatyām yaḥ aśvamedhena yajate iti ādi artha vāde vidhi kalpanam iti ced na avinā abhāvāt tathābhūta sādhana tvasya vidheya tva vyāpta tvāt vyāpaka anupalambha bādha udadvārāya vā prayojana abhāvāt na tad kalpanam tatra iti api āhuḥ 
TC_13.21–13.22^1	 yat tu iṣṭa sādhanatva abhidhāne karaṇe liṅgaḥ anuśāsanāt darśa paurṇamāsābhyām iti anabhihita adhikāra vihitā tṛtīyā na syāt iti tat na upāya tā mātra abhidhāne api tad viśeṣa karaṇa tva anabhidhānāt vastutastu abhihita anvaya labhyam yāga iṣṭa sādhana tvam iṣṭa sādhana tva mātrasya vidhi artha tvāt navyāḥ tu cikīrṣā dvārā jñānasya kṛtau hetu tā cikīrṣā ca kṛtau= icchā sanaḥ prakṛti artha gocara icchā vāci tvāt pipakṣa ādi vat na tu kṛti viṣaya pāka ādi viṣaye kṛti sādhya tva prakāraka icchā abhidhāyaka tvam pāka ādeḥ prakṛti anabhidheya tvāt na hi kṛti vācakasya tad viṣaya vācaka tvam karoti iti ukte tad viṣaya saṃśayāt evañca kṛta āviccheṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt vā vṛṣṭi ādau tathā kalpanāt yadā ca kṛtau= icchā tadā sā eva cikīrṣā anyatra icchā mātram na tu kṛti sādhya tā jñānāt kṛtau kṛti sādhya tva abhāvāt 
TC_13.22^2	 atha pākam kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchā anubhava siddhāḥ anubhava apalāpe upekṣaṇīyatva āpatteḥ sā ca kṛti sādhya tā jñānāt sā ca cikīrṣā pada apratipādya api kṛti hetuḥ samāna viṣaya tvāt na tu kṛti icchā kṛti hetuḥ kṛti viṣaya aviṣaya tvāt iti ced asti tāvat pāka kṛtau= icchā vṛṣṭī i= chāvat asti ca kṛti sādhya tva prakārikā icchā pāke tathā api kṛti icchā eva kṛti kāraṇam lāghavāt na tu kṛti sādhya tva prakārikā icchā gauravāt dhātu arthān uparakte kṛti svarūpe icchā eva na udeti iti ced na pāka ādi kṛti iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt pāka kṛtau= icchā tatas kṛtiḥ iti abhyupagamāt na ca avagati pravṛttyoḥ samāna viṣaya tvam ubhaya siddham tasya eva vicārya tvāt katham tarhi pākam kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchā yathā vahni sādhya tvena 
TC_13.23^1	 iṣṭa sādhana tā avagamāt vahninā pākam sādhayāmi iti icchā tathā kṛti sādhya tvena iṣṭa sādhana tvāt pākasya pākam kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchā anyathā tad tad upāya sādhya tvena icchā pāka ādau tad tad upāya sādhya tva prakāraka jñānāt syāt iti ananta kāraṇa kalpanā syāt mama tu upāya icchāyām iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam eva hetuḥ kriyā dvārā kṛteḥ iṣṭa sādhana tva jñāne kriyāyāḥ api iṣṭa sādhana tvam viṣaya eti kṛtī icchā bhavantī kriyā āviṣayā api bhavati iti jñāna icchā prayatnānām samāna viṣaya tā api atas eva pākam cikīrṣati iti cikīrṣā viṣaya tayā pākaḥ pratīyate yat vā icchā viṣaya viṣaya tayā pākaḥ pratīyate ita tasya karma tā grāmam jigamiṣati śatrum jighāṃsati iti atra grāma ādeḥ iva na hi grāma ādau= icchā siddha tvāt 
TC_13.23^2	 atas eva bhoge sukhe ca cikīrṣā tad anukula kṛteḥ iṣṭa hetu tvāt anyathā kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe tat cikīrṣā sāmagṣantaram kalpyate evañca sandhyā vandanam duḥkha sādhana avandana abhāva rūpa tvena iṣṭam tad sādhanam kṛtiḥ iti liṅgarthaḥ anyathā kṛtiḥ na kṛti sādhyā sandhyā vandanañca na iṣṭa sādhanam iti kasya kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tvam vidhi arthaḥ syāt atas eva eka pratyaya abhidheya tva pratyāsatteḥ antaraṅga tayā vidhi pratyaya abhidheya iṣṭa sādhana tvasya kṛtau= eva anvayaḥ na prakṛti arthe tathā eva cikīrṣā kāraṇa jñāna janaka tvāt prakṛti arthasya ca kṛtau viṣaya tvena anvayaḥ iti 
TC_13.24	 ucyate vahni sādhya tvena kṛti sādhya tvena vā na pākasya odana sādhana tā iti uktam katham tarhi vahninā pākam sādhayāmi iti icchā iti ced naḥ iṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāte yatra yat sādhya tvam jñāyate tatra tad sādhya tvena icchā bhavati iti yatheṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāte pāke vahni sādhya tvena avagate iṣṭasya sādhana tā jñānāt kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchā tathā ceṣṭā sādhana tvena kṛti sādhya tvena ca jñāte kṛti sādhya tva prakārikā icchā na tu iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna mātrāt iti 
TC_13.25^1	 acāryāḥ tu pravartakam iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam eva liṅga ṛtaḥ tu āptabhiprāyaḥ lāghavāt pākam kuryāḥ kuryām iti atra vidhi liṅgaḥ sambodhya sva kartṛka kriyā icchā abhidhāyaka tvenā jñā prārthanā śaṃsana ādi liṅgaḥ vaktra ādi icchā abhidhāyaka tvena liṅga mātrasya icchā vācaka tva kalpanāt ca evañca svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti asya svarga kāmasya kṛti sādhya tayā yāgaḥ yāga yatnaḥ vā āpteṣṭaḥ iti arthaḥ tatas yaḥ vyāpāraḥ yasya kṛti sādhya tayā yat vyāpāra viṣayakaḥ prayatnaḥ vā yasya āptena iṣyate sa tasya balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi iṣṭa sādhanam iti vyāpti grahāt yāgasya iṣṭa sādhana tvam anuminoti 
TC_13.25^2	 tathā hi yāgaḥ mad iṣṭa sādhanam mad prayatna viṣaya tayā āptena iṣyamāṇa tvāt yathā mad pitrā mad prayatna viṣayatayā iṣyamāṇam mad bhojanam mad iṣṭa sādhanam tathā āca idam tasmāt tathā evam na kalañjam bhakṣayet iti asya mama kalañja bhākṣa prayatnaḥ na āpta icchā viṣayaḥ iti arthaḥ tatas kalañja bhakṣaṇam mama balavat aniṣṭa sādhanam mad iṣṭa sādhana tve sati api āptena mad prayatna viṣaya tayā aniṣyamāṇa tvāt yathā mad pitrā mad prayatna viṣaya tayā aniṣyamāṇaṇam madhu viṣa sampṛkta anna bhojanam mama balavat aniṣṭa sādhanam tathā ca idam tasmāt tathā sa ca āptaḥ veda vyākhyātāḥ bhagavān īśvaraḥ eva 
TC_13.25^3	 yaḥ tu vede pauruṣeya tvam na upaiti tam prati vidhiḥ eva tau= aṅgarbhaḥ iva śruti kumāryāḥ puṃyoge pramāṇam na tarhi lāghavam tātparya gauravāt i īśvara ādi ananta kalpanāt iti ced na lāghava ādinā icchā bodhaka tvena loke liṅgaḥ pramāṇa siddha tvena phala mukha gauravasya adoṣa tvāt na tu kartuḥ asmaraṇam bādhakam prāk eva nirāsāt tṛptikām anayā viṣa bhakṣaṇa pravṛttasya viṣa bhakṣaṇam tat kṛti sādhya tayā na īśvareṇa iṣyate tatas viṣa bhakṣaṇasya īśvara icchā viṣaya tve api na tena vyabhicāraḥ yat vā ratkāma kṛti sādhya tvena yaḥ vyāpāraḥ āptena iṣyate sa tasya iṣṭa sādhanam viṣa bhakṣaṇañca tṛpti kāma kṛti sādhya tvena na īśvara icchā viṣayaḥ māna abhāvāt atas eva na kalañjam bhakṣayet iti atra kalañja bhakṣaṇam tṛptikām anayā bhakṣaṇa pravṛttasya kṛti sādhya tvena āpta icchā viṣayaḥ na iti tasya īśvara icchā viṣaya tve api viśiṣṭa niṣedhaḥ upapadyate abhiprāya vidhi pakṣe balavat aniṣṭa an anubandhi tva mānu mānikam iṣṭa sādhana tā vidhi pakṣe tu tat api śakyam iti gauravam iti 
TC_14.1^1	 atha svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti ādā= iṣṭa sādhana tvam kārya tvam vā yat vidhiḥ sa samabhivyāhṛta kriyā anvayī tad anyā anvayī vai atra guravaḥ na āhatya kriyā kārya tayā liṅgā bodhayitum śakyate svarga kāma niyojya anvaya yogya tā jñāna virahāt kāmanā viśiṣṭasya hi mama idam kāryam iti boddhṛ tvam niyojya tvam tat kāmanāyāḥ tad bodha upayoge sati bhavati sa ca kāmanā anantaram kāmya sādhana tā bodhanāt kārya tā bodhe sati syāt evañca svarga sādhana tā bodhe sati svarga kāma niyojya anvaya yogya tā na ca kāla antara bhāvi svarge kriyā sākṣāt paramparayā vā sādhanam iti śabdaḥ bodhayitum arhati āśu vināśi tvāt paramparā ghaṭakān upasthiteḥ ca tṛtīya prakāra abhāvāt ca anyathā tam ādāya sādhana tva sambhavāt kalpyam api apūrvam na syāt iṣṭa sādhana tā vidhi pakṣe sphuṭā eva anupapattiḥ kārya tā vidhi pakṣe anvaya prakāra tayā sādhana tvam śābdam iti phalatas na kaścid viśeṣaḥ 
TC_14.1^2	 atas kriyātas anyat svarga sādhanatā arham kriyā kārya tā nirvāhakam liṅga ādi arthaḥ nanu sva jātīye anvaya darśanam yogyatā dṛṣṭañca ghṛta pānasya āśu vināśinaḥ kāla antare puṣṭi hetu tvam iti ced na yathā kathañcid sājātyasya ayogye api sattvena yogyatayā avyāvartaka tva āpatteḥ padārtha tāvat chedakena sājāti asya ādya jātaḥ payaḥ pibati ityādau prakṛte ca asambhavāt tasmāt anvaya prayojaka rūpavat tvam sa ajātyam atas eva drava dravya tvam seka karaṇa tve prayojakam iti ayogyaḥ vahniḥ tad iha āśu vināśinaḥ kāla antara bhāvi phala janaka tve phala samaya paryanta sthāyi vyāpāra janaka tvam prayojakam atas apūrvam vinā sājātyam eva na gṛhyate ghṛta pānasya tu vaidya ka upasthita dhātu sāmyam ādāya puṣṭi sādhana tva yogya tā jñānam vijñasya atha bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvaḥ yogya tā na ca sādhana tva mātre bādhakam sākṣāt dbodhe api paramparā sādhana tvam ādāya tad viśrānti sambhavāt 
TC_14.1^3	 na ca yogyā anupalabdhā dvārasya bādhāt paramparā sādhana tvam api bādhitam saṃskāsya iva tasya sambhavāt anyathā vācye api apūrve kriyā kāmi kāryā na syāt kāmya asādha tvāt na hi yat eva ayogyam tad paścāt yogyam ayogya tve ca niṣphalaḥ prayāsaḥ na ca kāmi kāryam apūrvam tad arthi kāryā ca kriyā iti vācyam yāge rāgāt iti anena virodhāt tathā api dvāra anupasthityā paramparā sādhanam iti jñānam na bhavet iti ced satyam kintu svarga sādhanam yāgaḥ iti jñānam sākṣāt parampara uda āsīnam vastu gatyā paramparā sādhana tva viṣayakam utpadyamānam na ayogya tayā paribhavitum śakyam yadi ca sākṣāt paramparā viśeṣa dvaya vyatiriktam sāmānyam na asti eva tadā ananugamaḥ kim vā viśeṣayasi sākṣāt paramparayā vā iti na ca yāvat viśeṣa bādhe tat bidhitam paramparā sādhana tve abādhāt iti mā evam 
TC_14.1^4	 yogya tā hi sva bādhaka pramāviḥ aho vā sakala bādhaka pramāviraho vā ādye vahninā siñcati ityādau sva bādhaka pramāta dvirahau samaya bhedena staḥ iti tat eva yogyam ayogyañcā iti prāptam dvitīye tu yogyā anupalabdhā tat niścayaḥ aśakyaḥ para pramāyāḥ ayogya tvāt na ca vācyam sakala bādhaka pramāvirahar svarūpa sannā iva prayojakaḥ iti ayogye yogya tāmram ādanvaya bodha abhāva prasaṅgāt anyasya tatra bādhaka pramā sattvāt anvaya prayojaka rūpavat tvena bādhaka pramāviḥ aho niścīyate iti ced tarhi prāthamika tvāt sā eva yogya tā na ca sā prakṛte sambhavati iti uktam kiñca eka viśeṣa bādhe śābda sāmānya jñānam tad itara viśeṣa prakāra tā niyatam chidra bādhe chidra itara ghaṭa jñāna vat na ca dvāra anupasthityā prakṛte tathā ghaṭate etena yat uktam praśasta rūpavān caitraḥ iti atra gaura śyāma viśeṣān avagame api rūpa mātram avagamyate tadvat viśeṣān avagame api sādhana tva mātram iti tad pratyuktam tatra eka viśeṣa bādhā bhāvena audāsīni asambhavāt 
TC_14.2	 etena svarga kāma anvaya balāt kriyāyāḥ phala sādhana tvam tat balāt ca paṭoḥ saṃskāsya iva sthāyi tvam kalpyatām kim apūrveṇa saṅkalpa viśeṣasya yāgasya agre pratyakṣa anupalabdhi rātma viśeṣa guṇānām prathama kṣaṇaḥ eva sva viṣayaka pratyakṣa janana svabhāvāt astu na ca evam kriyā antaram api tathā pramāṇa abhāvāt evam loka prasiddha kriyā kārya tva vyutpattiḥ api bhagnāḥ na bhavati iti parāḥ tam svarga sādhana tā yogya tayā svarga kāma anvayaḥ tad anvaye ca sthāyi tvam iti anyonya āśrayāt lāke dharmi grāhaka mānena kriyāyāḥ kṣaṇika tva niścayāt ca 
TC_14.3	 nanu deva pūjā arthaḥ yajiḥ pūjā ca ārādhanāḥ gauravita prīti hetuḥ kriyāḥ atas devatā prīti dvārāḥ yāgasya svarga sādhana tvam prīteḥ kṣaṇika tve api prīti anubhava janita saṃskāra dvārā tad sambhavāt atas eva āgneya ādau prīti bhāgitayā agna gaderuddheśya tvam iti ced na yaj deva pūjāyām iti hi śābdika smṛtiḥ smṛti tvāt eva na svatas pramāṇam na ca yāgasya devatā prīti hetu tve svargasya devatā prīti sādhya tve vā māna antaram asti vastutas tu cetane deve mānam eva na asti yatra ca viṣṇu prīti kām a ādi vādaḥ asti tatra viṣṇuḥ eva prītiḥ na tu viṣṇoḥ ṣaṣṭhī artha lakṣaṇā doṣāt viṣṇu śabdasya prīti viśeṣa vācaka tvam vedaḥ eva kalpyate na ca devatā pūjā artha yaji anvaya balāt tathā anyonya āśrayāt nanu evam āgneyān dīnām ṣaṇām kṣaṇika tvāt yogyatā anavagatau parama apūrva kāraṇa tvānavagame katham apūrva kalpanā iti ced na kāmye apūrva vācya tva sthitau āgneya ādau tad vārā sādhana tvasya yogyatā sambhavāt na tu prathamam 
TC_14.4	 nanu yaḥ brāhmaṇāya avaguret tam śatena yātayet iti atra brāhmaṇa badha udyam asya śata yātanā hetutva avagame yathā durita apūrvam kalpyate tathā iha api iti ced na avaguret yātayet iti atra hetu hetum atorliṅiti anuśāsanāt liṅgāḥ avagoraṇa śata yātanayoṃ= niyatam paurvāparyam bodhyate pratyakṣeṇa anubhava smaraṇayoḥ iva tat ca sādhana tve sādhana sādhana tve vā ubhayam api madhya varti ghaṭitam iti dūrita kalpanam saṃskāra vat iha tu vidhi anuśiṣṭā liṅc kārya tām āha kiñca kāmī kāmyāt anyat kāmya avyavahita sādhana tayā jñātam eva kartavya tayā avaiti iti niyamāt na kriyāyām kāminā unvayaḥ yogyaḥ na ca tṛpti kāmasya pāke pravṛtteḥ vyabhicāraḥ odana kāmasya tatra pravṛtteḥ tṛpti kāmanā tu tad kāmanā upayoginaḥ na tu sākṣāt anyathā sādhana sādhane pravṛttiḥ na syāt kāmya sādhana tvam pravartakam 
TC_14.5^1	 lāghavāt iti ced na bhojana kāmasya siddhaudanasya pāke pravṛtti prasaṅgāt tasya odana dvārā bhojana sādhanatva aviśeṣāt viśeṣaṇe tu yatra avyavahita sādhanam pākaḥ tat na kāmyam yat ca kāmyam tatra na avyavahita sādhanam pāka eti na pravṛttiḥ nanu pākasya siddha odana dvārā bhojana sādhana tvam na sambhavati dvārasya asādhya tvāt odana antara dvārā ca tathā pratisandhāne avyavahita viśeṣaṇe api kutas na pāke pravartate odana antare dvāre sākṣāt sādhana tvāt iti ced na pākasya bhojana sādhana tve viśeṣasya aprayojaka tayā odana mātrasya dvāra tvāt tasya ca sādhya tvau= iva adāt odana viśeṣe ca siddhe odana kāmanā virahāt na tulya tvam 
TC_14.5^2	 nanu odane siddha tvāt yathā na kāmanā tatas eva dvāra tā api na atha odana antarasya asiddha tvam ādāya dvāra tā tarhi kāmanā api syāt tasya asiddha tvam ādāya dvāra tā tarhi kāmanā api syāt tasya asiddha tvāt iti ced na pākasya eka viśeṣa dvāra tā bādho na viśeṣa antara dvāra tā virodhī sakala viśeṣasya ekatra dvāra tva asambhavāt eka viśeṣa siddhau tu tanmātra kāmanā vicchidyate na hi sakala viśeṣa siddha tvena sāmānya kāmanā vicchedaḥ sakala viśeṣa siddheḥ asambhavena tad anuccheda prasaṅgāt atha vā kāmyāt anyat sākṣāt asādhana tvena jñāyamānam yat kartavya tayā kāmaḥ budhyate tad kāmya avyavahita sādhanam antarā kṛtvā eva yat vā kāmyāt anyat kāmaḥ prathamam kāmya avyavahita sādhanam kartavya tayā avaiti paścāt tad vārāḥ avyavahita sādhanam iti prathamam yāge kāmikārya tā bodhaḥ ayogya tā aparāhataḥ eva 
TC_14.6	 uttānāḥ tu vivāda viṣaya uliṅg samabhivyāhṛta kriyā anvita kārya tā bodhikā pramāṇa liṅga tvāt laukika liṅga vat liṅgapasthāpyam kārya tvam samabhivyāhṛta kriyā anvitam liṅupa sthāpi a kāryatva tvāt paceta iti kāryatva vat yāgaḥ vā kāryatva anvitaḥ kriyā kāryatva avagamena apūrvam kalpyam iti tatra prathame yāga anvita kārya tva bodhika tvam liṅgaḥ bodhyate na tu kriyate na ca yogyatā jñānam vinā tad sambhavati iti uktam eva na hi yogyatā ādikam vinā eva tad anumāna prāmāṇya prayojana mātrāt anvitam abhidhīyate śabdena na antyau kuryāt iti atra vyabhicārāt veda asya anuvādaka tā āpātāt ca 
TC_14.7^1	 nanu apūrve vyutpatti virahaḥ tathā hi prasiddhārtha svarga kāma pada samabhivyāhārāni atha anupapattyā upasthite śaktiḥ grahītavyā na ca śābda anubhavāt pūrvam apūrvam upasthitam māna abhāvāt apūrva tva vyāghātāt avācya tva āpātāt ca na ca liṅga ādinā tad upasthitiḥ vyutpatti anantaram tad pravṛttau= anyonya āśrayāt na ca kārya tvena upalakṣite tatra śakti grahaḥ upalakṣaṇam hi smaraṇam anumānam vā agṛhīte sambandha āgrahāt aśakyam iti mā evam kārye dharmiṇi kāryatvena śakti grahāt kāryatva viśiṣṭañca upasthitam eva tatas anvita abhidhāna daśāyām yāga viṣayakam kāryam iti anubhavaḥ svarga kāma anvayā yogya tayā ghaṭa ādikam tiraskṛtya kriyāṃbhinne yogya tā vaśā t yāga viṣaya ka apūrve paryavasyati na tu apūrva tvena śakti grahaḥ 
TC_14.7^2	 na ca apūrvam kāryam iti anubhavaḥ bhavati ca sāmānyatas sambandha buddhiḥ sahakāri vaśāt viśeṣa buddhyā payaḥ yathā tava eva kartṛ viśeṣa siddhiḥ nanu kāryatvena api kim ghaṭa ādau śakti grahaḥ uta apūrve ubhayatra vā na ādyaḥ anya pratipattau= anya śakti grahānupayogāt na antyau prāc anupasthiteḥ iti ced na yena hi rūpeṇa śabdena anubhavaḥ janyate tena rūpeṇa śakti grahaḥ padārtha smaraṇañca śābda anubhava hetuḥ na hi prameya tvena śakti grahaḥ padārtha smaraṇañca ghaṭa tvena śābda anubhava hetuḥ evañca ghaṭa ādau= eva kārye śaktā liṅgiti śakti grahaḥ tatas kāryam iti smaraṇam tatas yogyatā ādi vaśāt pracura dravya guṇa karmāṇi kāryāṇi vihāya yāga viṣayakam kāryam iti unubhavaḥ bhavan= apūrvam ālambate yogya tvāt ca tasya sthāyi tva lābhaḥ atas eva vākya artha anubhava mātra viṣaya tvāt tat apūrvam 
TC_14.7^3	 na ca smṛtānām ākāṅka ādi vaśāt anvaya bodhaḥ padena kriyate na ca apūrvam smṛti gocaraḥ iti vācyam śakti graha padārtha smṛti śābda anubhavānām samāna prakāraka tā mātreṇa hetu hetum at bhāva avadhāraṇāt lāghavāt āvaśyaka tvāt ca na tu kvacid sahacāra mātreṇa anvaya pratiyoginaḥ eva upasthitiḥ tathā gauravāt go padāt apūrva gavān anubhava prasaṅgāt ca viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya bodhe sarvatra tathā eva anyathā parvatīya vahniḥ vyāpaka tayā na avagataḥ iti katham tad anvayaḥ anumitau nanu sāmānya lakṣaṇā pratyāsattyā sarvāḥ eva vyaktayaḥ vyāpti grahe śakti grahe ca viṣayībhavanti katham anyathā parvatīya dhūma vyāpti agrahe tasmāt anumitiḥ iti ced na yena rūpeṇa vyāpti grahaḥ tena rūpeṇa vyāpya tvena vā pakṣa dharma tā grahaḥ anumitau kāraṇam astu kim tathā api ca sā yadi asti mama api na asti cetāvāpi 
TC_14.7^4	 kiñca tava darśane sā asti iti sutarām apūrvavācya tā kāryatvena hi rūpeṇa apūrvasya api śakti graha viṣaya tvam padārtha smṛti viṣaya tvañca na ca evam apūrva tva kṣatiḥ yāga viṣaya tva ādeḥ viśeṣasya kārye liṅgam vinā anupasthiteḥ yathā parvatīya tva bhānam vahnau na anumitim vinā nanu kārye yadi kriyā sādhāraṇena liṅga śaktiḥ kriyā ca ayogyā iti yogya pūrva lābhaḥ tadā nitya niṣedha apūrvayoḥ alābhaḥ na hi tatra ayogya tayā kriyā tyaktum śakyate phala aśravaṇāt kalpanā yāñca bīja abhāvāt na ca ekatra nirṇītaḥ śāstrarthaḥ anyatra tathā eva iti nyāyāt tatra api apūrvam eva liṅgarthaḥ iti tyaktum na hi apūrva tvena śakti grahaḥ kintu kāryatva viśiṣṭe dharmiṇi kriyā ca tathā bhavati eva na ca kāryeṇa samam kriyāyāḥ anvayān upapattyā apūrve paryavasānam 
TC_14.8^1	 abhedasya api anvayāt iti mā evam na hi loke paceta ityādau kārye dharmiṇi śaktiḥ kalpitā kintvananī alabhye kṛti rūpe kāryatva mātre dharmiṇaḥ pāka ādeḥ dhātoḥ eva upasthiti sambhavāt kriyā kāryatvasya anvitā abhidhāna labhya tvā tathā ca dharmiṇi vede śaktiḥ kalpanīyā sā ca kriyā nirāsena eva na hi kriyāyāḥ kāryatva anvaya yogya tve dharmiṇi śaktiḥ kalpayitum śakyate tasmāt ayogya tayā kriyā nirāsa anantaram tat atiriktaḥ eva śaktiḥ kalpanīyāḥ na ca kriyā atirikta kāryāt kārya mātram laghuḥ tatas kriyā api śakyā eva iti vācyam 
TC_14.8^2	 yatas na brūmaḥ kriyā atirikta kārya tvena śaktiḥ kintva yogya tayā kriyāyām nirastāyām dharmiṇi śakti kalpana samaye yat kriyā atiriktam tatra śaktiḥ na tu śakti grahe kriyā praveśaḥ na hi yad prayukta anupapattyā yat kalpanam tat eva tasya viṣayaḥ evañca kāryatvena api tad atirikta kārye eva śakti kalpanāt nitya niṣedhayoḥ api tat eva upāsana ādi anvaya yogyam liṅga abhidhīyate na tu kāryatva mātram dharmiṇi bādhaka abhāvāt lakṣaṇa aprasaṅgāt ca ghaṭa ādiḥ tu liṅga śakti grahe na tiraskriyate na puraskriyate uyayathā api gauravāt anvita abhidhāna daśāya anvayogya tayā tasya apraveśaḥ vidhi pratyayasya ca tatra aprayogaḥ kevalasya tasya asādhu tvāt dhātu samabhivyāhāra sthale ca tad arthena anvaya bodha janana niyamena ghaṭa ādi apratipādaka tvāt atas eva aprayogāt eva aprayogaḥ apūrva tvam vā prayoga upādhiḥ iti vadanti 
TC_14.8^3	 atha apratipādya dhaṭa ādi vṛtti tayā na kārya tvam pravṛtti nimittam pratipādya ghaṭa ādi vṛtti tayā na kārya tvam pravṛtti nimittam pratipādya mātra vṛtteḥ eva tathātvāt anyathā prameya tvam eva tathā astu iti ced na yad prakārikā hi pratipattiḥ pada janyā tat eva tatra pravṛtti nimittam phala kalpya tvāt śakteḥ na tu pratipādya mātra vṛtti sāsnādau vyabhicārāt na ca prameya tvam tathā tad bodhasya apravartaka tvāt atas eva lāke liṅc lākṣaṇikaḥ kriyā bhinne dharmiṇi vede śakti kalpanāt na ca laukikānām apūrve tātparyam sambhavati pūrvam pramāṇa antareṇa apratīte kriyā sādhāraṇa śaktau= api loke lakṣaṇā eva paceta iti atra hi pāka kārya tā avagamyate tatra kāryatve liṅgaḥ tātparyam lāghavāt 
TC_14.8^4	 na dharmiṇi kriyāyāḥ dhātu labhya tvāt tat āhuḥ tātparyāt hi vṛttiḥ na tu vṛtteḥ tātparyam iti tṛtīyāyāḥ karaṇa tva eka tvāt kāryam kāryatvañca na svatantram śakyam kintu viśiṣṭam viśiṣṭāt ca viśeṣaṇam anyat eva iti kāryatve lakṣaṇā na ca kāryatva viśiṣṭa dharmī upasthitau= api dharmi aṃśam apahāya kriyāyām kāryatva anvayaḥ astu kim lakṣaṇayā iti vācyam na hi itara dharmi gata tvena upasthitasya dharmi antarākāṅkā asti atas svatantra kārya tva upasthitaye dharmi antara ākāṅkṣā asti atas svatantra kārya tva upasthitaye lakṣaṇāḥ yathā puroḍāśa kapālena tuṣān upapacati iti atra puroḍā śarthitayā tad anvita tvena upasthitasya kapālasya na upavāpākāṅkṣā iti svatantra kapāla upasthitaye adhiṣṭhāna lakṣaṇāḥ 
TC_14.9	 na ca vyutpatti virodhaḥ na hi loke kriyā kārya tve śaktiḥ avadhāritā yena virodhaḥ bhavet kintu kāryatva mātre kriyāyāḥ dhātu labhya tvāt na ca dharmi antare śaktau= api tad bhaṅgaḥ tasmāt prakṛti artha anvita sva artha bodhaka tvam pratyayānām gṛhītam pratyaya arthaḥ ca apūrvam api iti na virodhaḥ astu vā loke liṅgaḥ kriyā kārya tve śaktiḥ tathā api tad bhaṅgam vinā eva nānā artha nyāyena vede dharmi antare śaktiḥ tām vinā svarga kāma anvaya asambhavāt 
TC_14.10	 anye tu paceta iti ādau dhātunā eva pākaḥ kāryaḥ abhidhīyate liṅc tatra tātparya grāhikā na tu śaktāḥ niyamataḥ tādṛśi eva tad prayogāt sāmānya śabdasya viśeṣa paratvañca na vṛtti antara nirvāhyam atas eva vartamāna tva ādau na laṅgā ādi śaktiḥ iti loke śakya grahāt na vyutpatti virodhaḥ iti tat asat liṅaḥ kārya tve aśaktau pacipadāt kārya tva jñāna anupapatteḥ yugapad vṛtti dvaya virodhāt na ca ajahatsva arthāḥ ubhaya sādhāraṇasya anupasthiteḥ iti diś 
TC_14.11^1	 yat vā jñāne padānām śaktiḥ śakya tvāt evañca liṅga padam ekatra uccāraṇe yogyatā ādi vaśāt yāga viṣaya kam stāyi svarga janakam kāryam iti ekam jñānam anubhava rūpam pracura dravya guṇa karma vilakṣaṇa viṣayam kriyate na ca evam nānā arthavat ekaika jñāne śakti grahāt ekaika viṣayaḥ anubhavaḥ bhavet na samudita viṣayaḥ iti vācyam śakti graha kāle ekatra uccāraṇaḥ iti viśeṣaṇa mahimnā tad sambhavāt nānā arthe tu pramāṇa abhāvena gauravena ca śakti grahe tasya apraveśanāt tathā api amīṣām samūha ālambanam syāt na tu parasparam vaiśiṣṭya jñānam iti ced na sā kāṅkṣa dharma dharmi gocara eka jñānasya eva viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt cana ca samūha ālambana sambhedaḥ tasya nirākāṅkṣa viṣaya tvāt 
TC_14.11^2	 astu vā upasthiteṣṭha gṛhīta asaṃsargeṣu sthāyi tva svarga janakatva kāryatveṣu śaktiḥ agṛhīta asaṃsargakasya api viśiṣṭa jñāna samāna śīla tvāt atas ukta nyāyena tāvat viṣayakam ekam jñānam liṅgpadena janyate evam eva alaukika artheṣu svarga ādi padeṣu śakti grahaḥ nanu bhavatu ukta prakāreṇa śaktigrahaḥ tathā api liṅpadāt yāga viṣayaka kārya anubhave satya pūrva lābhāt svarga kāma anvayaḥ sambhavati iti upapādaka pratisandhāne prasiddhārtha svarga kāma pada samabhivyāhārānyatha anupapattyā liṅgaḥ kārye śakti kalpanam na hi prathamam upapādaka pratisandhānam vinā artha āpattiḥ sambhavati na ca śakti kalpanāt pūrvam upapādaka śarīra niviṣṭam apūrvam jñātam iti ced tat kim yaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ upapādakaḥ pakṣa dharma tā balāt siddhyati tad pratisandhānam artha āpattau kāraṇam tathātve pūrvam gṛhīta mātrasya kalpyate 
TC_14.12^1	 kalpanā uccheda āpattiḥ tasmāt yathā sāmānyatobhojanasya pīna tva sambandha avagamāt upapādaka tarke sati kalpanātaḥ viśeṣa avagamaḥ yathā vā sāmānya śakta vyakti vācaka padena samabhivyāhāra vaśāt viśeṣa abhidhānam evam atra api kārya mātra vācaka tve kārya viśeṣa lābhaḥ sambhavati iti tarkita upapādaka pratisandhānāt bhavati artha āpattyā śakti kalpanam yāga viṣaya kañca kāryam na ghaṭa ādi tasya sa viṣaya ka tva abhāvāt viṣaya tvañca jñāna ghaṭayoḥ iva svabhāva sambandhaḥ vā tad nirūpaṇa adhīna nirūpaṇa tvam vā tad sāna saṃvita saṃvedya tvam vā vyāvṛtta sādhana tvam vā iti asti hi yāga dāna homa janyā pūrvāṇām tulya rūpa sādhana antara vyavacchedena pratyeka mātra janya tvam tat uktam viśabdaḥ hi viśeṣa arthaḥ sinotiḥ bandhaḥ ucyate viśeṣeṇa sinoti iti viṣayaḥ atas niyāmakaḥ iti 
TC_14.12^2	 nanu yena rūpeṇa śakti grahaḥ tena rūpeṇa kāryatva śakta āliṅg padāt lakṣaṇayā kārya upasthitau yogyatā ādi vaśāt apūrva lābhaḥ astu kārya smaraṇam hi anvita abhidhāna upayogi na tu apūrva smaraṇam tat ca padena padārthena vā iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ kāryañca śakya kārya tva sambandhi tayā avagatam eva iti ced na liṅgaḥ lākṣaṇika tvena apūrvān anubhāvaka tvāt na ca itara anvitasva artha śaktasya yajya ādi padasya itarat a pūrvam ādāya anubhāvaka tvam iti vācyam itara upalakṣita sva artha anvaya mātre hi padānām śaktiḥ na tu itaratra gauravāt pada antara labhya tvāt ca lakṣaṇa āyāñca tīra upalakṣita anvaya śāli sva artha anubhāvaka tvīm itarapadasya tīrasya tu saṃskārāt upasthitiḥ asat nihitena anvita abhidhāna abhāvāt na ca apūrvam saṃskāra viṣayaḥ kiñca yajipadena svarga kāma kārya viṣayaḥ yāgaḥ iti unubhava ubhavet lakṣaṇāyām itara padasya lakṣaṇīya viśeṣaṇa sva artha viśeṣyaka anubhava janaka tvāt na ca etādṛśaḥ bodhaḥ ākāṅkṣitaḥ na ca yāga aviśeṣita kārya mātreṇa svarga kāma anvayaḥ pratīyate kintu yāga viṣayaka kārya viśeṣe tathā ca tathāvidha bodha artham liṅgaḥ kārye śaktiḥ eva iti 
TC_15.1^1	 atra ucyate anvaya prayojaka rūpavat tvam na yogyatā anāpta ukte payasā siñcati iti atra sati api anvaya prayojaka drava dravya tve bādhaka pramāyām anvayā bodhāt atha yogya tve api sva bādhaka pramāyām anvayā bodhāt atha yogya tve api sva bādhaka pramāvirahar kāraṇam tarhi saḥ api avaśya apekṣaṇīyā eti lāghavāt sā eva yogya tā evañca tat eva yogyam ayogyañca syāt iti ced satyam yathā daśā viśeṣe tat eva sā kāṅkṣam anākāṅkṣam āsannañca tathā sva bādhaka pramāta dvirahadaśāyām tat eva anvaya bodhe yogyam ayogyañcā abhidhīyate sva bādhaka pramāyām tad virahe vā yogya ayogya tā vyavahāra darśanāt sva bādhaka pramāvira hadaśāyām yogyatā ādi sattve api vahninā siñcati iti atra anvaya bodhaḥ apramā doṣa vat puruṣaṇīta tvāt 
TC_15.1^2	 sāmānyabhānasya kiñcid viśeṣa bhāna niyata tvāt viśeṣa ābhāne katham tat bhāsate iti na vastu gatyā paramparā sādhanam viśeṣaḥ bhāsate evaya paramparā sādhanatvantu prakāraḥ na bhāsate tad prakāra bhāne hi paramparā ghaṭaka jñānasya hetu tvāt yathā ghaṭena jalam āhara iti atra yogyatayā chidra itara ghaṭe ghaṭa tvena bhāsate na tu chidretara tvena tathā sati lakṣaṇāyām yugapad vṛtti dvaya virodhena ghaṭān anvaya prasaṅgāt ubhaya sādhāraṇa rūpeṇa anupasthiteḥ ca na ajahatsva arthāḥ atha saṃskārāt tad u sthitiḥ na ca subvibhaktīnām prakṛti artha gata sva artha anvaya bodhaka tva vyutpatteḥ tatra vibhakti arthaḥ nāvyīyeta iti vācyam prakṛti arthaḥ hi prakṛti pratipādyāḥ lakṣaṇīya anvaya anurodhāt sa ca saṃskāra sahakārāt prakṛte api na ca tasya aniyata udbodhakāt na niyatā tad upasthitiḥ
